The Agenda of the World Economic Conference is Undecided 63

Monetary Issues May Be Considered First

Young Designated as US Chief Representative

▲National Telegraph, London, 19th: The order of discussion of the four major issues at the World Economic Conference has caused a headache for British and other national experts, because the situation has changed since the United States abandoned the gold standard. British experts initially believed that international trade restrictions should be discussed first, followed by stabilizing exchange rates, raising prices, and monetary and credit policies. The British feel that countries should not be asked to agree on monetary and credit policies until other issues are resolved. However, after meeting with US experts, the procedure was changed. Monetary issues will now be considered first. Although the actual discussions at the future meeting may not necessarily follow this procedure, some experts believe that the instability of the US dollar has seriously hindered Anglo-American trade, so monetary issues should be discussed first. Furthermore, major countries' efforts to stabilize exchange rates are expected to remove obstacles to tariff issues. As for prices, they have already risen. Looking at the current situation, the World Economic Conference may end earlier than expected. In short, currency and tariffs will be the two biggest issues at the conference. It has not yet been decided which should be discussed first.

▲Havas Telegraph, Washington, 19th: President Roosevelt is currently considering the composition of the US delegation to the London Economic Conference. The President seems likely to appoint Owen Young, who previously drafted the Young Plan, as the chief representative. Other representatives include California Republican Senator John Simes and former Secretary of War Baker.

Meeting of British and German Banking Leaders 64

▲Reuters, London, 19th: Dr. Schacht, president of the Deutsche Bank, passed through here this afternoon on his way back from the United States and plans to stay briefly to meet with Norman, governor of the Bank of England. Norman greeted him at the station. Dr. Schacht did not want to make any statements about his talks with President Roosevelt in Washington, as he must first report to the government.

▲Havas, London, 20th: People here are very interested in and also uneasy about the meeting between the president of the German central bank, Schacht, and the governor of the Bank of England. This meeting continues the talks that Schacht had in France and the United States, and is based on German foreign debt. This meeting is very important because it takes place before the German creditors' meeting on May 29. The situation of Germany's delayed transfers has caused unease in London banking circles. London banking circles criticize the National Socialist government, saying that it has never improved German finances and believes that Germany should first ask for a sacrifice on long-term loans. If short-term debts are also to be deferred, British banks must use rediscounting methods to assist bondholders. Therefore, people generally intend to relend to the German central bank in order to avoid the suspension of due debts.

Saito Visits Saionji 65

Reports on Internal and External Situation

Finance Minister Declares Intention to Remain in Office

▲United Press, Tokyo, 20th: Prime Minister Saito visited Saionji in Okitsu at 1 PM this afternoon and held talks for one hour. He left at 2:15 PM and took a car to Numazu to see the Empress Dowager. In the car, he told reporters that today's visit to Saionji was not to retain Finance Minister Takahashi. The decision of Finance Minister Takahashi to stay or leave is the responsibility of the cabinet and should not bother the elder statesman. He absolutely did not want such a method of shirking responsibility. However, the purpose of his visit to Saionji was to report on the truth of the May 15th Incident, Roosevelt's peace application, the progress of the Sino-Soviet Railway incident, countermeasures for the World Economic Conference, the current situation of the disarmament conference, the military situation in North China, and the internal situation of the domestic political situation. As for the issue of the finance minister's stay or departure, he will seek to meet with Takahashi for discussion in the near future after returning to Tokyo. The current situation requires him to stay in office, and he will certainly not disappoint the public's expectations. If Finance Minister Takahashi refuses to stay in office, whether he will step down to take responsibility cannot be predicted. He is not optimistic about the future, but he is not pessimistic either.

Japanese Fleet Reorganized 66

Navy Prepares Large-Scale Commemoration

▲Dentsu, Tokyo, 20th: The Navy will convert the temporary combined fleet into a standing fleet, under which the First, Second, and Third Fleets will be placed. This has been implemented today. At the same time, the Third Squadron of the First Fleet has been renamed the Seventh Squadron, the Fifth Squadron of the Second Fleet has been renamed the Sixth Squadron, and the First Overseas Fleet has been renamed the Eleventh Squadron. Furthermore, the warship Izumo, Tenryu, and the 27th Destroyer Squadron have been renamed the Tenth Squadron. Because of the changes in personnel, the commander of the First Overseas Fleet, Rear Admiral Sakano Tsuneyoshi, has been reassigned to the commander of the Tenth Squadron, the commander of the Fifth Squadron, Rear Admiral Ichimura Hisao, has been reassigned to the commander of the Sixth Squadron, and the commander of the Third Squadron, Rear Admiral Suzuki Giichi, has been reassigned to the commander of the Seventh Squadron.

▲Japan United, Tokyo, 20th: The 27th of this month is the Japanese Navy Anniversary Day. The naval authorities are planning to hold a large-scale commemoration to evoke a sense of tension among all the people because now is a time of emergency.

Peru-Colombia Dispute Resolved 67

▲National Press, Maima, 19th: The dispute between Peru and Colombia over the jurisdiction of the port of Leticia has been resolved. The details will be announced soon. This time, Colombian leader Lopez was invited to the Peruvian capital to discuss a resolution with Peruvian President Benavides. Leticia is a small port on the Amazon River, formerly an important rubber market, with a population of just over 1,000. It was ceded by Peru to Colombia in 1922, but last year, Peruvian unofficial troops, driven by nationalism, seized the port, and the Peruvian government then sent troops to follow up and refused to return it. As a result, the two countries have been fighting undeclared wars for months. Since the assassination of former Peruvian President Sanchez and the succession of the new President Benavides, policies have changed slightly, and they have finally been persuaded by neutral countries and the League of Nations to begin negotiations.

League of Nations Administrative Council 68

Increase Non-Permanent Directors

▲National Press, Geneva, 19th: The committee studying various proposals for the reform of the League of Nations Administrative Council decided today to increase the number of non-permanent directors by one, that is, from nine seats to ten seats, for a total of fifteen seats including the permanent directors. This new approach will be piloted for three years to allow representatives of countries that do not belong to any geographical or political group to join the Administrative Council. The German representative argued that it should be reconsidered before the end of the three years in order to find a way to change the current factional system. At the beginning of the establishment of the Administrative Council, there were four permanent and four non-permanent directors. Later, the number of non-permanent directors was increased to six and then nine, and now it is ten.

Nazi Rampage in Danzig 69

Ruling Party Issues Protest Statement

▲Reuters, Warsaw, 19th: The Danzig ruling party issued a statement today protesting the activities of the Danzig National Socialist Party, saying that the Nazi rampage endangers the existence of Danzig and demanding that Prussian state parliamentarian Leisemann be deported because he led a group of National Socialists yesterday to disrupt a meeting of the Danzig ruling party. Dr. Schim, Speaker of the Danzig Senate, intended to deliver a speech, but the meeting broke up. Dr. Rosting, the League of Nations High Commissioner for Danzig, arrived in Warsaw today to discuss the current situation in Danzig with the Polish Foreign Minister.

▲Havas, Warsaw, 19th: The conflict between the National Socialist Party and the National People's Party in the Free City of Danzig has become more acute. The National People's Party has fiercely criticized the National Socialist Party for occupying the Social Democratic Union, and the leader of the National Socialist Party said, "Since the National People's Party seems to be uniting with the Social Democrats to deal with our party, we can no longer cooperate with it, and we should also use the same method of dealing with the Social Democrats to overwhelm that party."

Sound Measures Already in Place for Security in Peiping and Tianjin 70

— It is Reached

Japanese Army Stops Advancing, Our Army Deploys New Defense Line

Huang Fu Says He Comes to Save the Nation With a Spirit of Sacrifice

(New Developments in the Northern Situation, People's Hearts Gradually Stabilizing)

Special dispatch from Beiping: The Japanese army's large-scale invasion of Shanhaiguan this time has several steps. The first step is to invade the major towns of eastern Luanhe, and the western parts of Shixia and Miyun, deploy troops in Shanhaiguan, and threaten Peiping and Tianjin. The second step is to buy off traitors to brew a puppet organization "North China State," while surrounding Peiping and Tianjin and stirring up the northern situation. However, their greatest purpose is not to directly occupy Peiping and Tianjin and make any displays of power. Their maneuvering and posturing are nothing more than to ensure their possession of the three northeastern provinces and Jehol and Chahar, and to complete their Manchurian-Mongolian policy. As for their main demands on us, the first is to sign an acknowledgment of the puppet "Manchukuo" and directly offer up tens of millions of square miles of land and people. The second is to delineate Peiping and Tianjin as political districts, with the Great Wall as the boundary, with mutual non-aggression. If one of the two is achieved, the goal has been reached. As for Shanhaiguan, there is no desire for the time being. They turn to capture Chahar and actively devote themselves to the development of the three northeastern provinces and Jehol and Chahar, realizing their Manchurian policy that they have never forgotten for decades. Now the first step of the plan has been completed, and the goal they hoped to achieve has also slightly deviated from their wishes. Therefore, since the previous day, the Japanese troops on all routes have stopped advancing and are waiting for the situation to unfold. Our country's policy towards Japan has always been one of resistance and negotiation due to the lack of national strength. Responding to the above, we have no choice but to change with the times and the location. Since the September 18th Incident, we have been making resistance in terms of strength, while seeking the support of international justice and fairness. The various countries are constrained by their own interests and the atmosphere of world unrest regarding the Sino-Japanese problem. They are reluctant to act for fear of the consequences, and the Japanese bullies have been rampant and lack of sanctions. Under this environment, our country can only strive for development with the sympathy of all countries in the world. Although the national strength is weak, it is absolutely difficult to accept the alliance under the city. It is extremely difficult to sign and acknowledge the "Manchukuo," even if only an inch of land and a single soldier are left. We can only maintain an attitude of non-compromise and non-peace, and seek a temporary peaceful solution under mutual understanding. Since the large-scale invasion of the Japanese army, the generals at the front have been able to work hard to fight against the powerful enemy. However, in this era of scientific warfare, flesh and blood are no match for the ruthless sharp weapon, resulting in the strong bandit penetrating deeply and Peiping and Tianjin feeling threatened. All parties feel that the security of Peiping and Tianjin is related to the safety of the entire country, and they must try their best to seek a policy of stability. A considerable method has now been agreed upon, and it may be nowhere for a while. Judging from today's situation, the northern situation seems to have a spring cloud spreading and gradually revealing a peaceful image, and the panicking hearts of the people are gradually stabilizing.

Huang Fu, the chairman of the Executive Yuan's Political Affairs Reorganization Committee stationed in Peiping, has had close talks with all parties in Nanjing and Shanghai after being ordered. On the way north, he also exchanged views with Lu Han, Ji Yu. After arriving in Peiping yesterday afternoon, he went to Jurintang to visit He Yingqin and discussed secretly for several hours. At 9 PM that night, he gathered key figures from the military and political circles in Peiping in Yiniantang to discuss the northern situation until midnight before the meeting adjourned. He met with the press this morning at 10 AM and made the following important remarks:

"What I personally wanted to say on this trip north was all mentioned when I passed through Tianjin. I just arrived in Peiping yesterday and am not yet fully aware of the situation in all aspects. People in the south only know that the situation in the north is serious. Only after arriving in the north did I realize how serious it is. My task, as the name implies, is to be a political officer. Regarding diplomatic affairs, the central government has repeatedly stated, and Mr. Wang Jingwei has also made many statements. I am dispatched here to handle everything in accordance with the central government's intentions. After the 17th year of the Republic, I lived at home in Mogan Mountain and did not ask about politics for six years. Old friends in the government often took the national affairs into consideration, and I politely declined because I did not dare to take on any positions again. This time, in view of the country's such a crisis, and the north where I have lived for more than 20 years, which is no less than my second hometown, because of historical and emotional reasons, I think this appointment is absolutely different from the previous situation. I came here with a spirit of sacrifice to save the country from danger. You in the north only know the severity of the air here. I don't know the hidden worries of the south. I recently went to Nanchang, where I learned that the communist situation is not only difficult to suppress, but is also growing day by day. The enemy in the north is so serious, and the hidden dangers in the south are also at risk of exploding. If we wait for the country to collapse before we start to remedy it, it will be even more difficult, so we must wait for it to collapse and first start to remedy a part of it. Knowing that it is a fire pit, we should also jump in first. The current situation can be set as an analogy, such as in a house, a heater is needed in winter and a fan is needed in summer. It is summer, and a fan is needed. The heater cannot be completely abandoned, but if the furnace continues to burn, it will be too hot to survive. The Political Affairs Reorganization Committee can also be established within ten days. In such times, it is not necessary to organize, and things can be done the same way to avoid the spirit being used for internal trivial matters," and so on. The war at the front has stopped since the day before yesterday. Our troops have all reached the planned defense line. The Japanese army has also stopped advancing. Xu Tingyao's military headquarters has moved to Beiyuan on the outskirts of Peiping today. The military headquarters of He Wansong and other armies have also been relocated. (18th)

Returning from the Front Lines 71

(1) Observations from Tianjin by Our Special Correspondent Geng Ya

Special dispatch from Tianjin: Our army at the Beining front began a westward retreat on the 13th at midnight. For several consecutive days, orders to garrison at a location were immediately followed by orders to retreat. Veterans of military life simply left their packed belongings at the station and did not venture elsewhere, constantly inquiring about train departure times to be ready to leave at any moment. As a result, the station was piled high with goods, often overcrowded. However, the troops retreating to Xugezhuang on the 14th had a rest for two days and nights. Although it was reported that Wang Yizhe's unit on the Pingyu Avenue, due to pressure from superior enemy forces (what the front-line troops called flanking maneuvers), had retreated from Fengrun (Xugezhuang belongs to this county) to the vicinity of Yutian, and the enemy continued to pursue, Wang's unit appeared to be continuing its retreat. Even on the mornings of the 15th and 16th, enemy planes had visited the skies above, circling and surveying. News of the enemy bombing Fengrun County also spread frequently. By the afternoon of the 16th, around 1 or 2 PM, refugees who had fled from the mining areas east of the village suddenly returned in disarray, their faces ashen with panic, saying that the situation in Tangshan was extremely chaotic. Around 9 or 10 PM the previous night, as our last retreating troops were leaving the station, countless traitors and rioters in yellow and gray, with mismatched clothing, emerged and caused disturbances everywhere. Those who resisted were harmed. We turned back and ran away, and so on. Once this news spread, the villagers were even more alarmed than before. People ran wildly, and many shops closed. As a result, rumors of continued retreat became even more rampant. It was said that the Wang and Weng-Zhang divisions, after bravely resisting the enemy and suffering heavy casualties, had no choice but to retreat. Villagers who carried wounded soldiers to this place witnessed the reality and were still willing to forgive them, praising them endlessly. The reporter, hearing of their noble deeds and admiring them, wished to detour to visit them, inquire in detail about the truth of the battle situation to share with readers, and fulfill the promise made earlier to meet the army commander and division commanders again on the front lines when they were encountered in Sanhe. Unfortunately, due to transportation issues, this was not possible. Furthermore, Staff Officer Yang of the 57th Army said that the war clouds were so thick that even Commander Wang might not know his location at any given moment. Thus, the reporter decided to join the refugees, who were as lost as stray dogs, crowding onto the night train back to Tianjin, which was packed beyond capacity. The journey was often delayed because military transport trains were stopped on various sidings to allow passage, causing delays that nearly doubled the usual train speed. The next morning (the 17th), at 9 AM, the reporter visited Chairman Yu of the Hebei Provincial Government, but because it was not visiting hours, the reporter exited and walked north along Jingyi Road. The roadside was full of pistol-carrying police officers, spaced about ten meters apart, and vigilance was especially high at intersections. Whenever a rickshaw moved slowly or pedestrians paused to watch, they were severely interfered with. Countless cars drove in a continuous stream, heading towards the new station. It was later learned that Huang Fu, Chairman of the Beiping Political Affairs Committee, would arrive in Tianjin this morning to go to Beiping. Subsequently, there was news of a bomb explosion. Although Mr. Huang was fortunately unharmed, the atmosphere in Tianjin, already tense as "the mountain rain is about to come, and the wind fills the building," was further shaken by this sudden noise. Fortunately, the military and police authorities, since the 15th (the night of widespread rumors of traitorous riots), had implemented strict precautions, and all district teams were notified to pay special attention. In the event of an incident, traffic on all four roads leading to the location of the incident should be cut off, and pedestrians and vehicles should not gather in large numbers in one place. Suspicious households and pedestrians should be inspected. 2. Ferry boats and cargo ships in the river should be prohibited from passing if necessary. 3. Extra protection should be given to telephone exchanges, power plants, and bridges. 4. Strict precautions should be taken against those who hide bombs. 5. Those who spread rumors to mislead the public and engage in reactionary speech should be strictly arrested to maintain public safety and stabilize people's hearts. Shops and markets were filled with Russian goods, and it was said that anti-Japanese goods had gradually disappeared. Customers were as lively as usual, but most were just wandering around, and few actually had money to buy goods. Money shops mostly kept copper coins, causing copper coins to soar in price. In the past two days, the exchange rate for foreign currency had dropped to more than forty copper coins per yuan. Since Japanese planes flew to Beiping for reconnaissance and news of the retreat of troops guarding western Luan County spread, many residents moved into the British and French concessions, followed by the Italian concession, while the Japanese concession had none and some were even moving out. Among those seen moving along the way, many were refugees from Beiping (since the discovery of Japanese planes in Beiping, daily sales of first and second-class train tickets from Beiping to Tianjin were three thousand yuan higher than usual) and from the front-line war zones seeking refuge in Tianjin.

Student , head , student , also saying already from east , our army wants to recover. starting , imminent , year old , receiving family, to prevent unforeseen circumstances. , studying, classes have not been suspended, and classmates, the, its fate, although this is trivial, it is also one aspect of the current state of the city. The crude establishment of the committee seems like it can be delayed. After the international judgment from the thirteen votes against one vote last year, to the forty-two votes against one vote in February this year, Japanese diplomacy has been isolated. However, in reality, our country has not received any real international assistance. In other words, it is difficult to hope that the League of Nations will impose economic sanctions on Japan. Both the United States and Russia, which the Japanese consider their hypothetical enemies, also seem reluctant to offend Japan quickly. These are the disappointments of our country towards the West, and also the successes of Japan. They greatly hope that our country will recognize that the West is unreliable and should still turn to them to jointly seek the so-called East Asia cooperation and Sino-Japanese friendship. Huang Fu Arrives in Beiping 72

— Jin

The Assassin at the Tianjin Station is Beheaded on the Spot

Releases a Statement Denying Compromise with Japan

Military and Political Leaders of Beiping Welcome Him at the Station

He Yingqin Summons Generals to Report on Military Affairs

Special dispatch from Beiping: Huang Fu, the newly appointed Chairman of the Executive Yuan's Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee, along with the director of the Secretariat, He Qi , Tao Lüqian, He Jiecai and others, a group of more than ten people, traveled north from Nanjing by train on the 15th night, passed Jinan on the 16th evening, and briefly delayed his trip to meet with Shandong Province Chairman, Han Fuqu. He then changed trains and continued north. On the morning of the 17th, at 9:40 AM, he arrived at the new Tianjin Station. At 1:30 PM, he departed from Tianjin and did not arrive in Beiping until 4:40 PM. A detailed account of Mr. Huang's journey north is as follows:

A Shock in Tianjin 73

Huang Fu arrived at the new Tianjin Railway Station at 9:40 AM on the 17th, where Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong and leaders of provincial committees and various agencies were present to welcome him. After disembarking, Yu and Huang rode in the same car, traveling along Dajing Road directly to the provincial government. Security was tight along the way, with security teams and military police holding pistols and broadswords, standing guard in the center of the road and on both sides. At 11 AM, Chairman Yu hosted a welcome banquet in the large reception hall of the provincial government to welcome Huang. At 1:30 PM in the afternoon, Huang and others took the original train to Beiping. As Huang's train arrived at the new station, a young man threw a bomb from the overpass at No. 21 Yangqi outside the station. The explosion was extremely loud, shocking the staff at the new station. Two soldiers guarding under the bridge were also stunned and fell. The bridge suffered minor damage. The young man who threw the bomb was captured by the patrol police and sent to the First Army Headquarters for interrogation at 10:30 AM. He identified himself as Liu Kuaisheng, sixteen years old, from Caozhou, Shandong, and worked as an assistant in a manure factory in Hedong. Although he firmly denied throwing the bomb, patrol police and military police witnessed it firsthand. Therefore, he was escorted near the new station at 12:30 PM and beheaded as a warning. Because he did not admit to throwing the bomb, no confession was made public. According to speculation, Huang Fu's trip north and the atmosphere of compromise with Japan in Beiping and Tianjin, may be the reason why the young man opposed compromise with Japan and threw a bomb as a warning. Some also said it was traitors taking the opportunity to create disturbances. There were various rumors. Also, next to Jiajia Bridge on Dajing Road in Hebei, there was a tea stall with a white cloth bag on the tea table and a villager sitting next to it. Just as Huang Fu was about to go from the provincial government to the station, military police were heavily deployed along the way, and security was tight. Initially, the villager was not noticed, but after martial law was announced and the villager still lingered, the military police went forward to check and found a bomb weighing forty pounds in the white cloth bag. The villager tried to escape but was subdued by the military police and sent to the First Army Corps Headquarters for interrogation.

Denies Compromise 74

Because Huang Fu's trip north was related to the issue of easing the situation in North China, the reporter rushed to Tianjin on the morning of the 17th. After Huang arrived in Tianjin, he issued a statement to the press, saying, "I have lived in the South for a long time and do not wish to be involved in politics. Recalling the winter of the 13th year of the Republic, when Mr. Feng Yuxiang led his troops back to Beijing and overthrew Cao Kun, I was ashamed to serve in the Regency Cabinet. That lesson is still fresh in my mind. Now, revisiting the old capital, I cannot help but feel a sense of the present. The Political Affairs Reorganization Committee cannot decide on a date to meet because all the members have not yet arrived. However, the work of the committee can be carried out at any time in contact with all the members. There is no need to wait for the establishment of the Political Affairs Committee. I will follow the Central Government's consistent policy of negotiating while resisting to deal with the critical situation in North China. Only through the joint efforts of all parties can the national crisis be averted. Rumors that I will compromise with Japan after arriving in Beiping are absolutely untrue. I believe that at this time, no one in China dares to compromise with Japan. I have not been to Beiping and Tianjin for many years and do not know the current situation. I will first go north to observe the actual situation before determining the reorganization of political affairs in North China. Minister He (Yingqin) is responsible for military matters, and I can also participate with my opinions. Negotiations with Japan cannot be achieved in just a few words or half a day. Local issues in North China cannot be negotiated locally. Everything must still be presided over by the Central Government. As for stabilizing the hearts of the people in North China, I very much want to achieve this goal, but if there is no practical demonstration, it will not be beneficial. I am not confident about this, so I will not speak rashly. Rumors that military agencies in Beiping and Tianjin will be relocated to create a buffer zone between China and Japan are untrue. I think this is unfounded talk and is inaccurate."

Grand Arrival in Beiping 75

The reporter left Tianjin with Mr. Huang at 1:30 PM and did not arrive at the East Railway Station in Beiping until 4:40 PM. Deputy Foreign Minister Liu Chongjie, Military Council members Jiang Bocheng, Zhang Qun, Wang Shuchang, Beiping Mayor Zhou Dawen, Public Security Bureau Chief Bao Yulin, Acting President of Beiping University Xu Songming, President of Tsinghua University Mei Yiqi, President of Normal University Li Zheng, representatives of the Education Association Yu Shiyuan, professor of the Law and Commerce College Yang Zongpei, and Wang Wenjin, Lu Dingxin, Gao Lingbai, Ji Qingqian, Ma Manqing, Wang Zhixiang, Zuo Zonglun, Zhou Zechang, Zhou Quan, Guan Yanlin, Pan Yongjin, etc. were all at the station to welcome him. The Military Council had also dispatched a company of guards and a platoon of Central Military Police to guard inside and outside the station. From the East Railway Station to Zhongnanhai, the Public Security Bureau dispatched additional bicycle squads to guard the route. After Huang got off the train, he shook hands and thanked each of the welcomers, then left the station and drove directly to Jurentang in Zhongnanhai to visit He Yingqin, the acting chairman of the Military Council. After talking for about an hour, he returned to Fengzeyuan to rest.

Consultations on Military and Political Affairs 76

After resting briefly at Fengzeyuan, Huang went to Nanhai Jurentang to visit He Yingqin. They had a confidential discussion until about 6 PM before leaving. At 7 PM, He hosted a banquet at Jurentang to welcome Huang, inviting Jiang Bocheng, Wang Kemin, Zhang Qun, and others to accompany them. After the banquet, Huang invited He Yingqin and others to Fengzeyuan for a meeting to exchange preliminary views on the important issues in North China. That night, He also telegraphed Song Zheyuan, Pang Bingxun, He Zhuguo, and certain other important generals in the front lines, ordering them to come to Beiping immediately to report on the latest situation in the front lines and discuss everything. It is expected that the generals will arrive in Beiping on the 19th. Huang decided to convene a meeting of all members of the Beiping Political Committee at Fengzeyuan on the morning of the 18th to discuss the organization of the Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee. Huang also scheduled to meet with reporters at Fengzeyuan at 10 AM that morning to report on everything. (18th)

Grim Prospects for Shantou's Silver Industry 77

(Establishment of a White Certificate Management Committee)

Correspondence from Shantou: Shantou's silver industry has been greatly shaken in recent days. Several major silver firms have collapsed one after another. On the 13th, a run on the Tongyu Silver Firm on Haiping Road occurred. The firm had issued 40,000 yuan in banknotes. Fortunately, the Silver Industry Mutual Aid Society provided a sufficient amount of cash to rescue it, averting a grounding. Furthermore, Maotai Grain Store on Fuping Road declared bankruptcy on the 12th, owing a large amount to the street. Baosheng , which owes more than 700,000 yuan due to bankruptcy, has entrusted important figures in the business community to mediate with the debt group. The initial intention was to repay 80% of the debts, but the creditors refused. It is now said that they have agreed to repay the debts in full within one year, divided into four installments. Furthermore, 110,000 yuan of paper money white certificates of Fuan Firm has already had the full amount of money advanced by other firms, turned over to the Chamber of Commerce for redemption, and is gradually recovering paper money and white certificates on the market. The city's money supply is now extremely scarce. The Chamber of Commerce has requested that the Bank of China and the Provincial Bank allow merchants to borrow against real estate to facilitate turnover. The Bank of China must wait for orders from its Shanghai headquarters before daring to release the loan. The Chaozhou silver firms jointly issued 450,000 yuan in white certificates (10,000 yuan each) as an emergency measure. At present, white certificates are prevalent in various markets in Chaozhou and Shantou. The Shantou Exchange Bureau established a White Certificate Management Committee, with the following regulations: "Article 1: This committee is named the Shantou City Exchange Industry Association Guaranteed White Certificate Management Committee. Article 2: The purpose of this committee is to rescue the city's financial market and consolidate the credit of white certificates. Article 3: This committee shall be composed of seven members elected by the general assembly of the Exchange Industry Association to handle all matters of this committee. However, when reviewing property and evaluating prices, the city government and the Chamber of Commerce shall be invited to participate in order to ensure prudence. Article 4: The guaranteed property for the guaranteed white certificates issued by the firms of this committee shall be limited to shops, houses, and open spaces within the city area. The seashore is not guaranteed. However, after the price of the houses and shops is assessed at the current market price, it shall be discounted by 60%, and the open space shall be discounted by 40%. The review and registration procedures are as follows: (1) Registration; (2) Plaque; (3) Notation on the contract. The detailed measures for the above three items shall be determined by the Property Management White Certificate Guarantee Committee. Article 5: If the guaranteed property of each firm falls in value or suffers accidental loss during the period of validity of the white certificate, and this committee believes that the amount guaranteed by the firm is insufficient, the firm shall be ordered to supplement the original amount with other property. Otherwise, the amount of the white certificate shall be reduced. If the firm fails to comply, this committee shall report to the general assembly and terminate the joint guarantee agreement with the firm. Article 6: Each firm in this committee is free to decide whether or not to issue guaranteed white certificates. However, the amount of guaranteed white certificates issued by each firm shall be limited to a minimum of 10,000 yuan and a maximum of 50,000 yuan. The face value of each certificate shall be limited to 100 yuan. Article 7: Within the Property Guarantee White Certificate Joint Guarantee Association, if any firm goes bankrupt, the firms that have issued guaranteed white certificates shall contribute funds in proportion to the amount issued to redeem the certificates. Before the property is auctioned off and the funds are returned, a monthly interest of 1% shall be charged on the advanced funds to ensure fairness. Article 8: The issuance of guaranteed white certificates by this committee is only for temporary relief. The period is limited to three months. They are not redeemable. Every five days, the firms will mutually inspect the certificates to prevent counterfeiting. The matter will be discussed when the period expires. Article 9: These regulations of this committee shall take effect after being passed by the general assembly. Article 10: If there are any deficiencies in these regulations of this committee, they may be amended by the general assembly at any time." (14th)

Jiangsu Provincial Government Reduces Cocoon Industry Business Tax 78

(Temporarily Collecting 0.2% by Imitating Zhejiang Province's Example)

Correspondence from Zhejiang: The business tax for the cocoon industry in Jiangsu Province was originally stipulated to be 0.5% of business turnover. The provincial government, recognizing that the cocoon industry this year is not prosperous, specially made adjustments to reduce the tax in consideration of the hardships faced by merchants. The provincial government has now decided at a meeting to imitate Zhejiang Province's method and temporarily collect the tax at a rate of 0.2%. The Department of Finance has drafted collection methods and ordered the business tax bureaus in various counties to follow them. The methods are as follows: (1) Because of the quality of cocoons in this province, the cocoon industry business tax is temporarily collected at a rate of 0.2% of business turnover, imitating the methods of Zhejiang Province. (2) The cocoon industry business tax is of a temporary nature. In accordance with the provisions of Article 12 of the Business Tax Regulations, the value of the goods purchased should be used as the amount of business income, and the business tax should be collected uniformly. (3) Cocoon industry business tax should require the cocoon firms to record the number of dried cocoons returned in detail and pay the tax on behalf of the owners according to the number of bundles. (4) The value of each bundle of dried cocoons this year should be determined by the business tax bureau through market prices, verified and calculated, and reported in advance for record. (5) When opening a cocoon firm, in accordance with the cocoon firm regulations, it should report to the county the number of cocoon stoves and the amount of cocoons to be dried, and obtain a cocoon firm stove permit before being allowed to open for drying cocoons. At the beginning of this year, each cocoon firm should first register with the business tax bureau and apply for an investigation certificate, and then take the investigation certificate to the county government to apply for a cocoon firm stove permit for verification and to prevent tax evasion. The investigation certificate issued by the business tax bureau is specifically for verification purposes and does not cost any money. (6) The cocoon industry association should be responsible for assisting in the verification of the business tax paid on behalf of the cocoon firms. (7) Business tax supervisors and the Public Security Bureau should effectively assist in the collection. (8) The business tax bureau should temporarily assign investigation and collection staff to go to various cocoon firms to verify and collect taxes, and should carefully verify when the cocoon bales are exported to prevent tax evasion. (9) Cocoon industry business tax should be reported and paid separately, and the tax collection receipts used should be kept and returned for verification. (20th)

Citizens in Fuqing County, Fujian Province, Protest Taxes and Go on Strike 79

(Businessmen in Fuzhou Oppose Arbitrary Valuation of Shop Taxes)

Correspondence from Fuzhou: Since Fujian Province implemented an increase in business tax rates, disputes have repeatedly arisen with merchants. A strike occurred in Xiamen the month before. Recently, a similar strike occurred in Fuqing County, which is under the jurisdiction of Fuzhou Prefecture. All the county's tax bureaus were destroyed, and the situation is particularly serious. The details are described below:

Fuqing is a large coastal county, and many people go abroad to make a living. Commerce is quite prosperous. On the morning of May 6th, the county's business tax bureau sent staff to various businesses to collect business taxes, wanting to increase the tax rate of the Guanjingdou Qianfeng Rice Store, from 2 yuan and 7 jiao per month. The store owner, Liang Zhengqiao, refused to increase the tax, and a dispute occurred. The collecting officers said he was resisting taxes and arrested him, beating him along the way, causing his head to bleed. Onlookers were indignant. After Liang Zhengqiao was interrogated at the bureau, he was sent to the county government for detention, and a team was sent to Qianfeng Rice Store to destroy it and seal it up. This aroused public anger, and the Guanjingdou stores first announced a strike, which quickly spread to the entire city. Hundreds of people gathered and went to the business tax bureau on Pujie Street, dragging out the bureau chief, Zhang Damin, and staff members Song Zhiqian and Wu Hongtong, beating them severely, causing serious injuries. The objects in the bureau were also taken out and burned. At the same time, the slaughter tax bureau, stamp tax bureau, tobacco and alcohol tax bureau, deed tax bureau, and weights and measures inspection station were also destroyed. Each store's entrance was adorned with a paper flag, saying that they would not open until the tax corruption was punished. The silk, Beijing fruit, Jiangsu-Guangdong, fish, and meat trade associations jointly telegraphed the provincial party headquarters, provincial government, and pacification headquarters to report that the business tax bureau had illegally sealed shops, arbitrarily detained and beaten merchants, that public anger was aroused, and that the entire city was on strike, requesting that the situation be stopped to prevent the unrest from escalating. The party, government, and military agencies immediately telegraphed the county's security team, the county government, and the county party headquarters to quickly stop the situation. On the 7th, a joint party, government, military, and business meeting was held to persuade the merchants to open their shops first, and a temporary curfew was announced to prevent reactionary elements from taking the opportunity to cause trouble. Zhang Damin, the current director of the business tax bureau, went to the province for medical treatment on the 8th and reported the details of the incident. The Department of Finance immediately sent Rao Jingzhong to Fuqing on the 9th to investigate.

Furthermore, the merchants in Fuzhou also complained that the property tax bureau collected taxes not based on rent but arbitrarily valued the properties, forcing the merchants to pay. Often, the rent for a store was only a dozen yuan, but the value was estimated to be dozens of yuan, or twenty-odd yuan was estimated to be over a hundred. If they did not pay, they would be accused of concealing taxes and detained with a fine. For example, the Huazhen Jewelry Store on Nandajie Street was fined a huge sum of over 1,700 yuan. A delegation of merchants was organized on the 10th to petition for improvements in the property tax. More than a hundred representatives were elected and went to the county chamber of commerce, asking the chamber of commerce members to go to various agencies to petition. Because no one in the chamber of commerce was responsible for receiving them, public anger arose, and the chamber of commerce building was destroyed before they left. The joint meeting of the research institutes of each shop has now decided that the property tax should be collected based on the amounts recorded in the rent books and account books, and vowed to deny any arbitrary valuation. Yesterday, the property tax bureau issued a leaflet again, ordering merchants who had not paid the taxes to go to the bureau for recognition within two days, or they would be arrested. (12th)

The Economic Bankruptcy of Rural Shanxi and Suiyuan 80

Shanxi Provincial Bank Notes Equivalent to Waste Paper

Farmers Cannot Obtain Loans Despite Offering High Interest Rates

Taiyuan Dispatch: In this autumn of nationwide production decline and financial stagnation, the economic bankruptcy of rural areas is almost ubiquitous. However, the severity of the situation is most pronounced in Shanxi and Suiyuan provinces. In Suiyuan, years of drought, bandit harassment led by Wang, excessive land tax, and commercial decline have caused the market price of notes issued by the Suiyuan Official Currency Bureau to plummet repeatedly, resulting in a financial crisis on the verge of collapse. Although there was a good harvest last year, low prices hurt farmers and did little to improve people's livelihoods. As for Shanxi, it is due to the impact of years of turmoil, the excessive burden on the people, and the Shanxi Provincial Bank's issuance of sixty to seventy million yuan in banknotes, which were eventually redeemed at a rate of twenty yuan for one, rendering them almost entirely worthless. Various places also have to accommodate guest troops, and there are countless exorbitant taxes and levies. People in Shanxi have always been known for their business acumen, but recently, businesses outside the province have all stopped lending. Not only can they not absorb external wealth, but most of the unemployed cannot find a way to make a living. In addition, in recent years, the number of people addicted to "golden elixir" and morphine has remained high, spreading throughout the province, with an annual outflow of no less than tens of millions of yuan. Therefore, the economic bankruptcy and desolation of Shanxi today is truly unbearable to describe. People in remote counties and villages are especially impoverished, with no place to sell their produce. If they try to borrow money, even with interest rates as high as 8% or 10% per month per yuan, there is nowhere to borrow. Even loans from ordinary merchants require interest rates of 5% or higher, but there are still no transactions. The suffering endured by the people of the Republic of China is even more severe than natural disasters. Yan Xishan previously offered rewards for essays to solve this problem, soliciting public opinion to provide relief. Yesterday, he telegraphed provincial governments and county magistrates in distant provinces, ordering them to investigate the actual conditions in their respective areas, submit detailed relief measures within twenty days, so that [relief could be administered]. The original telegram is as follows:

To County Magistrates: I have personally inspected the construction of light railways and personally spoken with villagers, and I am deeply aware that financial stagnation is rampant everywhere, turnover is sluggish, interest rates are high, and farmers feel deeply pained. Inquiries into the causes and relief measures have revealed extreme complexity. It is difficult to obtain appropriate and effective solutions without widely adopting public opinion. Each county magistrate is close to the people and has more direct knowledge. Moreover, there are many insightful people in the countryside. I hope you will investigate the actual conditions in your county and propose relief measures or solicit opinions from people in the countryside, and submit them all to the office within twenty days, so that they can be combined with the solicited essays for consideration. It should be known that today's politics are different from the past. Apart from daily efforts to plan economic construction for the people, there is no such thing as "politics" for officials. I hope you will painfully eliminate the rigid habits of empty politics, concentrate your efforts on the economic aspect to alleviate the people's difficulties. I have been anxious about this matter for a long time. You must pay special attention and not delay in the slightest. This is my earnest hope. Yan Xishan (dated the 12th) Printed (the 14th).

Anhui Province Develops Water Conservancy and Adds Railways 81

Water Conservancy Project Plan Formulated

Construction of Wuhu-Zhe Railway Begins

Wuhu Communication: The Jiangxi-Jiangxi Engineering Bureau reported that the embankment works undertaken by the various district engineering bureaus were nearing completion. However, the aforementioned projects were mostly for disaster prevention, while economic construction should focus on promoting benefits. After the recent water disasters and bandit troubles, production has declined, and the way to remedy this lies in focusing on water conservancy and reviving the countryside. A complete water conservancy project plan has been specially formulated and submitted to the National Economic Commission for overall consideration and approval. However, due to the vast area under its jurisdiction, the bureau fears that it may not be comprehensive enough, so it has sent a general letter to the competent authorities along the river to investigate the following points: (1) Which river sections are most closely related to people's livelihood, what is their length, and how should they be dredged or straightened? (2) Where should culverts be added or gates constructed? (3) Where should revetment projects be built due to turbulent currents? (4) How should the protection and management methods of various embankments be regulated and implemented so that they can be preserved permanently? (5) How should the areas with accumulated water and lower elevation on both sides of the river be reclaimed to become fertile land? (6) What is the planting situation of agricultural products in various places, and is there a need for organization? (7) Have the embankments built by the people in the past been fully completed? What are the reasons for those that have not been restored, and how should they be remedied?

Wuhu to Wanzhi already has the old base of the Ningxiang Railway. However, the section from Wanzhi via Xuancheng to Sunjiabu, which is about 50 kilometers long, still needs to purchase land from the people for construction, which requires a large amount of money. The chief engineer, Hong Shen, has already gone to Shanghai to pass it through the board of directors. As for the steel rails to be used for the railway, 2,000 sections have also been negotiated with Germany and will be shipped to China in about two months. The five locomotives purchased from the Beining Railway have arrived in Pukou a few days ago and will be transported to Wuhu Jiangkou Station for storage within days. The Xuanwu Motor Company, which originally operated on this road, has now changed to the Xuanzhang line. The road also has a plan to imitate the Jingwu road and pave all the stones, which requires about 80,000 yuan in labor and materials. Liu Yiyan, the head of the Anhui Construction Department, specially took a car from Wuhu to inspect the road today. (14th)

Shanxi Province Builds Two Light Railways 82

(Completion of Datong-Tongguan Railway Project)

Taiyuan Correspondence: Last winter, Shanxi Province established the Shanxi-Suiyuan Ordnance Road Construction Bureau and the Ordnance Road Construction Training Institute, as well as a purchasing committee and other agencies, to prepare for road construction. Xie Zongzhou, the former head of the Pinghan Railway Bureau, was entrusted to handle the matter. At present, the Yuanping section from Taiyuan to Gouxian in northern Shanxi and the section from Taiyuan to Jiexiu in southern Shanxi are each about 300 li long. Soldiers have been dispatched by the troops stationed along the route to start construction. It is expected that both sections will be completed by the end of this year. After these two sections are connected and opened to traffic, they will continue to be extended in different directions, northward to Datong, directly to PingSui, and southward to Tongguan, connecting to Longhai, completing the planned Datong-Tongguan Railway. In addition to this main line, there are also plans for multiple branch lines, westward to Zekou bordering Shaanxi, and eastward to Jincheng bordering Henan, which will be built in sequence. Regarding the various materials required for road construction, in addition to those manufactured by the Renshen Manufacturing Plant, which was reorganized from the old ordnance factory in this province, the remaining items that cannot be manufactured have been ordered from foreign manufacturers separately. A few days ago, various foreign firms sent personnel to Bing to bid for the contract. After the contract was concluded and the purchase was made, the Ministry of Railways, when it recovered the Zhengtai Railway, planned to use the surplus funds from Zhengtai to repair this route in order to unify the railway administration. A preparatory office for the Datong-Tongguan Railway was established in Yuci, and a foreign engineer, Bo Yan, was appointed as the director to plan in Bing. While in Bing, Bo had several discussions with Yan Xishan and Xie Zongzhou. In order for Yan to formally contact the Central Government and explain Shanxi's plan to build a light railway to avoid misunderstandings, he sent Cui Tingxian, a senior counselor of the Suiyuan Appeasement Office, to Beijing with the entire plan to discuss with the Ministry of Railways. Cui arrived in Beijing and has already been there for over a hundred days. It is reported that a proper agreement has been reached, the main road will still be built by Shanxi Province with military labor, but all engineering plans, etc., will be guided by the Datong-Tongguan Railway Bureau of the Ministry of Communications. The Ordnance Road Construction Bureau in Xiyuan will build other branch lines separately. Cui will return to Bing to report and Yan inspected the actual construction of the sections that had started construction. A few days ago, he personally inspected the northern Shanxi section, and yesterday morning he accompanied Xie Zongzhou and Zhang Zhixin, a counselor of the Suiyuan Appeasement Office, and others, taking cars to inspect the southern section projects in Yuci, Taigu, Qixian, Pingyao, Jiexiu, and other counties. It will take about three or two days before they can return to the province. (12th)

Songjiang

Investigation of Basis for Levying Fishing Tax 83

Caoking in Punan is a coastal area, and most of the villagers are engaged in fishing. A few days ago, a team claiming to be the First Detachment of the Yangtze River Provincial Water Patrol ordered each fishing boat to pay a flag fee of 30 yuan. Fishermen went to inquire and said that it was reorganized by the Fishery Administration Bureau's Guard and Patrol Team. Because the fishermen could not afford to pay, they opened fire twice and collected 60 yuan, issuing a triangular flag. The matter was known to the county government, which ordered the Public Security Bureau to send Chief Inspector Chen to thoroughly investigate. No official documents for fee collection by the Water Patrol Team were found, and no notification was given for assistance. Therefore, a notice was sent to the team to suspend the collection temporarily, and the matter will be handled after the county government receives clear instructions for assistance.

Dispute Over Silver Content in a Gold Chain 84

Rifeng Silver Shop in Fengle Bridge is a century-old store with a good reputation. The ornaments sold by the shop are marked with a pattern. Yesterday, Xia Yongming, an employee of Quanda Pawnshop, brought a gold chain that was not pawned to exchange. The shop assistant recognized that the chain was indeed produced by the shop. When weighing and paying the price, the shop owner suddenly suspected that the chain was suspicious and might be mixed with other metals, so it should be tested by cutting. After obtaining permission, a base metal was found mixed in the cut part. Xia was shocked and argued with each other. Both parties reported to a branch office. Patrol Officer Liu persuaded them gently. Because both parties were decent businessmen, this matter was related to reputation, he asked them to mediate and settle the case in writing. It is unknown how the counterfeit ornaments with the Rifeng logo originated, which is quite suspicious to the general public.

Suzhou

Opposition to Collecting Fishing Construction Fee 85

The Ministry of Finance is collecting fishery construction fees for Taihu Lake in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and has established a Taihu Lake Fishery Construction Fee Collection Office in Suzhou to announce the collection. However, this construction fee is borne by each fishing household, and each fishing household is scattered everywhere, so the collection is entrusted to each fish market, which will collect and remit it to the collection office. The fish markets believe that the fishing households are poor and unable to bear the burden, so they refuse to collect it on their behalf and have submitted a report to the Ministry of Finance for approval. Yesterday (20th), the Fish Market Association specifically notified the industry to postpone the collection on behalf of the fish markets before receiving the Ministry of Finance's approval. It is reported that the fisheries in various counties along Taihu Lake have also expressed the same opinion.

Fengxian

Difficult to Exempt Slaughter Special Donations 86

The Meat Industry Association previously received an order from the county government forwarded from the Provincial Construction Department to collect a quarter of the special slaughter donation as a special construction fund. However, the slaughter tax is collected from merchants. Due to years of famine and commercial depression, the pork market is bleak. It is already difficult to collect the regular and supplementary taxes under the education special fund. If the construction donation is increased again, it will be even more difficult. Therefore, a report was submitted to the county government, requesting that it be reviewed and forwarded. Recently, a reply was received, stating that the special fund is of utmost importance and should be collected in accordance with regulations to report.

Wuxi

Night Robbery Case in Nanyanshi 87

There is a Baishi Temple near Guhong Bridge in Hongshengli, District 11 (Nanyanshi) of the county, with five or six old and young monks. At about 1:00 a.m. the day before yesterday, a boat suddenly came, with eight or nine bandits on board, holding weapons and landing on the shore in a swarm. They opened the small door on the east side of the temple and entered, tied up all the monks, beat them severely, and forced them to reveal where the silver was hidden. Then they searched arbitrarily for an hour before escaping with their loot. After checking, it was found that silver, clothes, and other items worth more than 300 yuan were robbed. At the same time, Hua Sanlin's family in Huajiawan, Tangkou 396, in the same district, was also robbed by six or seven bandits from Jiangbei, who broke into the house and robbed more than 300 yuan. Wu Dexin, the director of the Public Security Bureau, dispatched detective team leader Dai Shouquan, with detectives, to investigate everywhere because of the frequent robbery cases in urban and rural areas. Yesterday, Detective Dai captured a robber named Pan Gen outside the North Gate Gongbei Building, who had robbed Hu Shengquan's family in Bujia Bridge, and took him back to the bureau for interrogation.

Wuxi fellow villagers in Suzhou initiated the organization of the Wuxi Fellow Association in Suzhou in order to connect the hometown friendship. Then they searched and looted all the clothes and cash, etc. Later, they heard a very urgent gong nearby and then fled away with their loot.

The Jiang'an coast of Tongyi was breached by high tides, and the situation is dangerous. Rugao

Lover Flees Home in a Heated Affair 92

There is a Lu who opened a sauce garden south of the General Temple outside the North Gate of Rugao. His wife, whose maiden name is a local of Chahe, has a small stature and a slender figure. After marrying Lu, she was still considered harmonious. They had four or five children one after another. Recently, she suddenly changed her usual state and always went out on the pretext of not returning. There are rumors everywhere, and Lu has heard something about it. However, because of his face, he euphemistically persuaded her. Not only did she not know how to repent, but she intensified. She actually lived with her lover. When Lu saw this situation, he still pretended to be deaf and dumb, hoping that she would repent. Unexpectedly, she fled alone in the early morning of the 16th, while her husband and children were asleep. The eldest son and the youngest daughter looked around for their mother. Now, in addition to sending someone to Chahe to report to her family, Lu also reported to the official government, requesting a manhunt.

Pinghu

Japanese Warships Patrol the Sea 93

Two Japanese warships came to the sea outside the Tianfei Palace in Zhapu, and sailors landed on the shore. In the name of buying fruit, they went along the road where they traveled, drawing the highway routes, tax police posts, and fort positions in the book before boarding the ship and driving away. Unexpectedly, three more ships came the night before, lined up with the previous two in the sea, shaped like a blockade. At night, they used deep-sea lights to illuminate the sea until they left. The residents are uneasy.

Encountering Bandits and Being Killed Midway 96

Xu Decheng, a villager in Shuangju Township, District 10 of the county, who is 28 years old this year, took a boat to the home of a relative in Zhengdu Town the day before yesterday to celebrate. Before he had gone more than a mile, he suddenly encountered a bandit boat carrying six or seven bandits, who ordered him to stop and jumped onto Xu's boat. After searching for a long time, they only found a few silver dollars. The bandits ordered him to take off his padded robe, but Xu refused to comply, which angered the bandits. They immediately raised their guns and fired at him, hitting his chest. He died immediately. It was truly tragic.

Xiaoshan

Reduction of Field Tax by Eight Percent This Year 97

The field tax in Xiaoshan County has been too heavy since the 20th year, with each mu of regular and supplementary taxes at 1.2 yuan per ten people, resulting in a sharp drop in land prices. County Magistrate Zhang, considering the burden on the people, specifically proposed at the previous county administration meeting to reduce the security regiment's share by 8 cents per mu for the 22nd year's grain tax. In addition to reporting to the Provincial Department of Finance for record, he ordered the grain counter to prepare and implement it.
