City News

Mayor Wu Returned to Shanghai from Beijing Yesterday Morning 98

Local Armistice Talks in North China Impossible

Factory Inspection Negotiated by Municipal Government

Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to Find Ways to Relieve Mexican Overseas Chinese

Mayor Wu Tiecheng, who previously went to Beijing to contact important officials, has now completed his official business. He returned to Shanghai from Beijing on the night express train at 8:00 a.m. yesterday. The reporter of this newspaper specially interviewed him at the Municipal Government yesterday. Wu absolutely denied the possibility of local armistice talks in North China. The record of his conversation is as follows:

Situation in North China 99

The reporter first asked about his observation of the situation in North China and the rumors of local armistice talks. Wu resolutely replied that, judging from the current situation in North China, the rumors of compromise, etc., are all fabricated by the other side. As for the armistice talks, he also believes that they are absolutely impossible. The Japanese army's current temporary truce is, on the one hand, necessary for military reorganization, and at the same time, due to President Roosevelt's declaration expressing a firm attitude and being completely consistent with the League of Nations, the Japanese side is ultimately concerned. As for the safety of Peiping and Tianjin, he believes that although the Japanese army has no intention of peeking for the time being, it will eventually use traitors to actively disrupt the situation.

Factory Inspection 100

Regarding the issue of the inspection rights of factories in the concessions, which is related to the entire labor administrative sovereignty of our country, the Municipal Government will never give up. While in Beijing, he repeatedly consulted with the authorities of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. It was decided that within the scope of not damaging our country's sovereignty and maximizing the protection of labor welfare principles, the Municipal Government will be responsible for starting negotiations with the Bureau of Works and frankly discussing a cooperative approach.

Postal System Issues 101

As for the Postal Economic System Research Association, the discussion on the postal economic system reform plan has been basically determined after several meetings. Only the issue of personnel after the merger of the Savings and Remittance Bureau has caused slight differences in opinion between the two sides, resulting in a temporary suspension of the meeting. While in Beijing, he repeatedly met with Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Transportation to exchange views. It has now been decided to start with the mediation of all parties to make the opinions of all parties tend to be consistent, and then continue the meeting. Minister Zhu is scheduled to come to Shanghai at the end of this month, and the meeting is expected to be convened at that time.

Relieving Mexican Overseas Chinese 102

Regarding the Mexican anti-Chinese incident and the measures to relieve Mexican overseas Chinese returning to the country, he also discussed and decided on measures with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission in Beijing. In terms of negotiations, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will send high-ranking officials to Mexico to seriously negotiate with the Mexican government to thoroughly resolve the issue. As for relief, the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission will send personnel to Shanghai to work with the local authorities to find ways to deal with the resettlement and repatriation of overseas Chinese returning to Shanghai, and the government and private parties will allocate funds to maintain the livelihood of the expelled overseas Chinese.

○ ○ ○ ○

Sun Ke Denied Compromise Between China and Japan Upon Returning to Shanghai Yesterday Morning 103

Temporary Truce on the Front is a Natural Trend

We Will Never Give Up Our Long-Term Resistance Policy

Sun Ke, the President of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing at 8:00 a.m. yesterday with his mother. Reporters from various newspapers specially interviewed him at his residence on Columbia Road yesterday. Sun firmly denied the rumors that China and Japan were about to compromise and said that the current temporary truce was caused by the international atmosphere and natural trends. A record of Sun's conversation is as follows:

Denying Compromise 104

Sun first said that since Huang Fu, the chairman of the Political Reorganization Committee stationed in Peiping, went north, the atmosphere of peace was strong, but the rumors that China and Japan would compromise, etc., were not credible. The government has long made concrete decisions on the military issue of resisting Japan, but unfortunately, it cannot be fully implemented due to various reasons. As for the telegram from Peiping stating that a truce method will be discussed under mutual understanding, he had not heard of it while in Beijing. In short, China and Japan will never compromise.

Temporary Truce 105

The current international atmosphere has changed suddenly since President Roosevelt's declaration was issued. Japan is therefore concerned and dare not rashly attack Peiping and Tianjin. Our side is also temporarily unable to counterattack due to strategic relations. All these reasons may create a de facto truce. However, this situation is temporary and not permanent. The creation of this situation has nothing to do with the resolution of major issues, nor is there any understanding or agreement.

Peiping and Tianjin Safe 106

Regarding the safety of Peiping and Tianjin, the Japanese army has gradually advanced in recent days, and the situation is becoming more and more serious. However, according to Sun's talk, although the situation in Peiping and Tianjin is becoming serious, war is not likely to break out. However, disguised occupation, such as secretly sending traitors to take advantage of the opportunity to riot and disrupt public security, is difficult to predict.

Southwest Issues 107

The Central Government is determined to resist Japan and suppress bandits, so it has consulted with the Southwest authorities to assist in suppressing the Gan bandits. After repeated discussions, it has been decided that the leaders of the Southwest will cooperate to assist the Central Government in suppressing the remnant bandits in Jiangxi Province within a short period of time. Although national affairs are urgent, there is nothing that cannot be done. Chen Mingshu, the former Minister of Transportation, has returned to China and transferred to Fujian from Hong Kong. It is reported that Chen will temporarily live in Fujian.

Xinjiang Disputes 108

The Central Government has sent Huang Musong to Xinjiang to handle the disputes. Huang was unable to leave immediately due to illness and will be able to leave in a few days. As for the issue of the reorganization of the provincial government in the province, the Muslims have expressed dissatisfaction with the current provincial government, and reorganization may be possible. At present, the actual situation in the province is difficult to understand due to the lack of direct reports due to poor telegram communication. Xinjiang is an important place in the west, with a large area and abundant resources, which cannot be ignored. It is hoped that the people and government of the country will pay attention to the development of the border areas. As for the war in Sichuan Province, which broke out again in the midst of national disaster, it is very hateful.

Drafting the Constitution 109

Regarding the drafting of the constitution, Commissioner Wu Jingxiong and others are responsible for carrying it out, and the first draft is about to be completed. As for the provision in the draft constitution that active servicemen shall not be appointed as presidents, a decision has not yet been made and is under study. Legislator Zhang Zhiben is unable to go to Beijing immediately due to various reasons, but his resignation has long been withdrawn.

National Congress 110

The Provisional National Congress has been scheduled to be convened in Beijing on July 1, and representatives from various places have been elected one after another. It is hoped that the Southwest will send representatives to Beijing to participate at that time. As for the rumors that the Southwest will convene a separate conference, there is no actual report and it is believed to be untrue.

Long-Term Resistance 111

Because of the many rumors in recent days, the reporter asked Sun whether the Central Government had abandoned its previous long-term resistance policy. Sun replied that it had not been abandoned and would resist to the end. However, at this time, internal unity is urgently needed to jointly plan the progress. As for the rumors that the Japanese side intends to prevent the government from supporting the anti-Japanese guerrillas and that they will all be eliminated, Sun said that they are not true. All the Northeast Volunteer Army that can form an army have been reorganized by the Central Government into formal troops. The rest are still guerrillas who have not formed an army, or are not accepted for reorganization, or the government is unable to reach them, and there are also those who do not listen to orders, but their strength is also very weak.

Song's Department Firmly Defends the Telegraph from Peiping and Tianjin 112

Xiao Zhenying telegraphed from Peiping, saying: (Title omitted) To all gentlemen, in recent days, the various troops in eastern Luan have been retreating step by step and are in a state of collapse. Song's department of the 29th Army has reluctantly obeyed repeated telegraph orders. On the one hand, they are struggling to support and cover the retreat of all parties. On the other hand, they are strictly controlling the last front line of Peiping and Tianjin. Our army has fought bloody battles for two months, sacrificing more than 10,000 people, but due to environmental constraints, all previous achievements have been abandoned. The soldiers are grief-stricken and almost unwilling to live. No matter how difficult it is, we must defend Peiping to prevent the enemy from fleeing south. Respectfully reported, Xiao Zhenying bows down.

Sheng Yuezhuang, a Representative of the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army in Jehol, Arrives in Shanghai to Report on the War 113

Yang Dianhua's unit, the 8th Route Commander of the Anti-Japanese National Army in Jehol, which is currently stationed in the Zhangjiakou area, is unwilling to be oppressed by the enemy and has gathered the people to rise up and resist Japan. After many fierce battles, they have repeatedly won great victories. Recently, they have also established contact with the 41st Army and will prepare to counterattack. Recently, they sent a representative, Sheng Yuezhuang, to Shanghai to report the truth to all walks of life. Sheng will be stationed in Shanghai on a regular basis and insists on not soliciting donations from the outside world.

Patriotic Youth You Long Abandons Home to Go North to Resist Japan 114

Mr. You Yinqiao of Guangdong, has a long-standing reputation in Shanghai's business circles. He has only one son, named Long, also known as You Hua, aged twenty-two. He graduated from St. Francis Xavier's College and is proficient in both Chinese and English. He is married with a three-year-old son. You Long works for a trust company, earning a considerable monthly income, and his family life is quite pleasant. However, Mr. You is filled with patriotism. Since the outbreak of Japanese aggression against our country, he has been filled with grief and indignation, vowing to join the army and fight the enemy, but unfortunately, he had no opportunity. During the January 28th Incident, Mr. You also worked in the rear. Recently, Luanzhou fell and Tianjin and Beijing are in danger. Mr. You, being young and passionate, felt even more enraged. Therefore, a few days ago, he secretly left his family, claiming he was going out, and went north to join the army. His family noticed he had been gone for many days and became extremely anxious. Then, yesterday, they suddenly received a letter from him from Beiping, only to learn that he had gone north to join the army and was attached to the First Training Team of the Weng Army. He will soon depart for the front line, and advised his family not to worry, saying he will only return after killing all the Japanese invaders.

Dependents of General Li's Officers Temporarily Stay in Shanghai 115

Ms. Xie Yiqing, wife of General Li Du, Commander-in-Chief of the Jilin Self-Defense Army, arrived in Shanghai the night before last. According to Liu Piguang, Li Du's representative in Shanghai, the dependents of the officers of Li's army will remain in Shanghai temporarily due to crowded trains. All food and lodging issues will still be taken care of by Qu Wenliu and Feng Yangshan, representatives of the United Association for the Relief of Northeastern Refugees stationed in Peiping. As for Mrs. Li Du, she has decided to stay in Shanghai to await General Li Du.

Chen Tiesheng of the Ciyou Association Goes North for Disaster Relief 116

Previously, with the fall of Yuguan and the subsequent fall of Rehe, the refugees in the war zone were suffering immensely, especially women and children. The Shanghai Chinese Ciyou Association, responsible for caring for orphans, could not bear to stand idly by. The association's executive committee appointed Zhao Jinqing (Chairman), Li Ting'an, Zhu Lide, Fei Wusheng, and Chen Tiesheng to form a War Zone Orphan Relief Committee. Chen Tiesheng was sent to Miyun, Changli Haiyang Town, Qinhuangdao, and Luanzhou to unite with local political, business, and religious leaders to organize shelters and establish Ciyou branch associations. He also worked with enthusiastic people from all walks of life in Peiping and Tianjin, such as Zhou Dawen, Yong Jianqiu, Zhang Boling, Chilton, and Qu Wenliu and Feng Yangshan, representatives of the Shanghai Charity Organizations' United Association for Relief of Northeastern Refugees stationed in Peiping, to plan for contingencies in the event of further developments in the situation. After completing his work, he returned to Shanghai and reported the situation and the conditions in the war zone to various organizations and groups, which garnered much sympathy and substantial financial assistance from various quarters. Recently, as Peiping and Tianjin become increasingly dangerous and the number of refugees increases, Mr. Chen has decided to go north again today for emergency relief. When necessary, he plans to send Wang Guan to provide guidance on educational affairs in various locations.

The Date of the Soviet Russian Inspection Group's Trip is Still Far Off 117

Affected by Russia's Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway and the Threat to Peiping and Tianjin

Two Matters Must Be Resolved Before Finance Minister Song Can Return to Make the Trip Possible

The Ministry of Industry, in conjunction with the industrial and financial circles of Shanghai, is preparing to organize a Soviet Russian Industrial Inspection Group to visit Soviet Russia to inspect the latest state of Soviet Russian industry in order to prepare for expanding trade with Russia. This matter has already been discussed and settled in Beijing by Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, and Bogomolov, Soviet Russian Ambassador to China, and preparations are underway to organize the group. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency visited relevant personnel of the Ministry of Industry yesterday to inquire about the details. According to the response, this matter is still affected by other factors, and the date of its realization will be after the autumn coolness. The details are as follows:

Organization: It was stated that since the severance of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, trade between the two countries has stagnated and been seized by other countries, which has been detrimental to both sides. After China and Russia announced the resumption of diplomatic relations, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry initiated the organization of this group, on the one hand to prepare for trade with Russia, and on the other hand to learn from the Soviet Russian experience to revitalize our country's industry. On the government side, personnel will be sent by the Ministries of Industry and Finance, while private industrial and financial groups can participate freely at their own expense. It is now heard that the city's Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, and those engaged in import and export, such as the soybean, silk, tea, and timber industries, are all willing to join the group and go for inspection.

Influence: This matter, after the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, could have been realized earlier if a Sino-Russian commercial treaty could have been signed smoothly. However, recently, because Soviet Russia disregarded the treaty and sold the Chinese Eastern Railway, jointly owned by China and Russia, to the puppet Manchuria, this act greatly hinders Sino-Russian relations. Therefore, the consultation on the Sino-Russian commercial treaty has to be delayed, which indirectly affects the inspection group. Moreover, the Japanese army is constantly invading, and Peiping and Tianjin are in imminent danger. The state of the country is so precarious that the progress of the inspection group cannot proceed as desired.

Implementation: The inspection group is expected to be costly, and the Ministry of Industry cannot bear it alone. It must wait for Finance Minister Song to return to the country to plan the funds before it can be realized. Currently, Finance Minister Song is on his way to England and there is no definite date for his return. Furthermore, the aforementioned military and diplomatic issues must also be resolved. Waiting for all matters to be settled, the estimated date for the trip to Russia for inspection is expected to be after the autumn season.

Japanese Police Interfere with Customs Officers' Inspections, Customs Protests Verbally 120

The Japanese Consulate Has Ordered Corrective Measures

The Dagong News Agency reports: The Chief Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs, Mr. Maze, has recently received reports from foreign customs officers that armed police dispatched by the Japanese Police Department at the Hongkou Mail Steamer Wharf have been acting tyrannically, obstructing customs personnel from carrying out inspections, and causing much hindrance to customs inspection duties, requesting that the matter be addressed and corrected. After investigation, it was confirmed to be true. The Chief Commissioner of Customs Maze sent personnel to the Japanese Consulate General the day before yesterday to lodge a verbal protest, demanding that all unreasonable interference by the Japanese police be stopped to avoid hindering customs inspection duties, because the Japanese police at the wharf not only do not assist customs personnel, but often prevent customs officers from searching Japanese mail steamers and the luggage of Japanese passengers. Such a situation is extremely unreasonable and should be corrected. After receiving the report, the Japanese Consul General summoned the Chief of the Japanese Police Department, Mr. Hanari, to inquire about the situation. In addition to deciding to reprimand the Japanese police for arbitrarily interfering with customs officers' actions, the Consulate General also dispatched several senior police officers to patrol the wharves in shifts to assist customs personnel in performing their duties at any time. If it is found that Japanese police are protecting passengers and obstructing inspections, they will be severely punished without leniency.

University Professors Joint Association Advises the Soviet Government 121

Based on Treaties and Facts

Explaining the Pros and Cons, and the Higher Meaning

Opposing the Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway

The Shanghai University Professors Joint Association held its seventh standing committee meeting yesterday at 3 PM. Zhang Shouyong, Zhang Jixin, Lin Zhongke, Kang Xuanyi, Qiu Hanping, Jiang Zhensan, Li Shengwu (Qiu as proxy) were present. Zhang Shouyong chaired and Kang Xuanyi recorded. Matters discussed included: (1) A draft letter to the Russian Ambassador to be forwarded to the Soviet Government was amended and passed. (2) Adding members to the Education Funding Independence Movement Committee. It was resolved to add twelve people, including Li Shizeng. (3) A letter of thanks to Committee Member Xi Wei for soliciting prizes for the essay contest. (4) Revising the methods of benefiting members. (5) The cultural introduction and other three forms were handed over to the investigation section. (6) A letter from Zhongwai Bookstore requesting an introduction to the eye-witness account of the fall of Rehe, which was handed over to the document section for handling. (7) The association's proposal to hire legal counsel will have its candidates re-examined. The association issued the following letter to the Russian Ambassador to be forwarded to the Soviet Government:

Your Excellency the Soviet Ambassador to China, and please forward it to your government: Relations between China and Russia were interrupted for several years, and both sides suffered losses in their interests. Later, due to the demands of the international situation and the urging of public opinion, and with the efforts of diplomacy, we were able to restore friendly relations. The people of both countries rejoiced and earnestly hoped that we could work together hand in hand to seek the welfare of mankind. Unfortunately, within less than a month of the restoration of diplomatic relations, the ambassador's credentials had just been delivered, and the commercial treaty had not yet been negotiated, your government announced the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, which has greatly disappointed our country and is deeply regrettable. The Eastern Railway is an economic enterprise jointly run by the two countries. Eighty years after the railway's completion and opening to traffic, the railway industry will be transferred to Chinese ownership without compensation. Within thirty-six years, China has the right to redeem it at a price (see Article 12 of the Sino-Russian Railway Company Contract of 1896). The Sino-Russian Agreement of 1924 also solemnly stipulated that the future of the Eastern Railway depends on China and Russia and that no other country has the right to interfere (according to Article 7 of the agreement). Furthermore, according to Article 4 of the agreement, the governments of China and Russia solemnly declare that they will not conclude any treaties or agreements that harm the sovereignty and interests of the other party. All these facts have treaties as evidence, and there is no room for unilateral destruction. The unilateral reasons held by your country are nothing more than that our country failed to participate in the administration of the Eastern Railway after the September 18th Incident, and thus lost its rights and position in the Eastern Railway. This kind of argument is greatly contrary to your country's consistent policy. Japan temporarily seizes our country's territory with violence, which all countries regard as illegal, while your country calls for supporting small northern ethnic groups and advocates international peace. How can you want to assist Japan while our country is resisting Japan with all its might? I don’t know how you will justify your actions. This action not only affects our country's sovereignty, but also your country will lose sympathy in the international community. If your country believes that temporary violent seizure can become a permanent legal occupation, then the Paris Peace Conference after the European War could have maintained the original state before the war, and the map of Europe would not have needed treaty revision. Alsace and Lorraine would not have needed to be returned. Even when your country was in the midst of revolution, it did not participate in the administration of the Eastern Railway for a long time, but our country did not use this to deny your country's rights. When the Eastern Railway Incident occurred in 1929, your country also sent an ultimatum stating that our country could not unilaterally dispose of the Eastern Railway. The words are still fresh in our ears, but now you are going back on your word, contradicting yourself, and making things worse, from disposition to sale, which has never happened before in history and must not be taken by your country. Even if your country recalls its previous words, how will it explain itself? The International Postal Union is seeking ways to resist the postal transport of the puppet organizations, but your country is now selling the railway, which is tantamount to helping the tiger do evil and is deeply disliked by the wise. I guess that the reason why your country has taken this wrong approach is to avoid conflict between Japan and the Soviet Union in order to maintain peace in East Asia, but in fact, it only increases disputes. The sale of the Eastern Railway will definitely become a major disaster for your country's national defense, and the threat will become even greater. Since the outbreak of Japanese militarism, the government's budget has long been stretched thin due to its excessive military spending, which has exhausted the people's resources. How can it have the surplus funds? The reason why it is willing to collect huge sums of money to contribute to the Chinese Eastern Railway is nothing more than that the country is using this to liquidate the old debts of the Tsarist regime. If your country falls into this trap, it will be tantamount to creating troubles for itself and shaking the foundation of the country. Our association carefully considers and weighs the pros and cons, and dares to offer sincere advice. I hope that your country will not cause endless disasters for a moment of temporary peace, and that Sino-Russian relations will not repeat the same mistakes. Please quickly forward this message to your government, and according to the founding policy of your country, resolutely abandon this extremely wrong proposition, which will not only be the good fortune of the future of China and Russia. With all due respect, The Shanghai University Professors Joint Association of the Republic of China.

Meeting of Representatives of Overseas Chinese Refugees from Mexico 122

It Was Resolved to Organize the Mexican Overseas Chinese Relief Association

Establishing Overseas Chinese Factories as a Radical Relief Measure

Hiring Xu Shiying, etc. as Fund Custodians

Representatives of the Overseas Chinese Refugees Delegation from Mexico, Huang Zhulin, Lin Wenli, Lin Huiyao, etc., in order to seek fundamental relief for the refugees, specially convened the first meeting of the delegation yesterday afternoon at 3 PM at the Dasanyuan Restaurant. All the representatives attended and unanimously elected Huang Zhulin as chairman. After reverently reading the Premier's will, they began to discuss the proposals. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded as follows: (A) Reporting Items: (1) Chairman Chiang sent a telegram donating 10,000 yuan. (2) The Central Relief Committee donated 2,000 yuan. (B) Matters for Discussion: (1) Representative Huang Zhulin proposed, "Establish the Preparatory Office of the Mexican Overseas Chinese Relief Association" immediately, please submit the proposal for discussion and resolution. It was resolved to pass it and stipulate the following measures: (a) Establish the preparatory office immediately and appoint Huang Zhulin as director. (b) Publish a statement in the newspaper and notify all overseas Chinese refugees to join the association and register for free, so as to find ways to maintain it. (c) Rent the third floor of No. 124 Guizhou Road as the preparatory address. Before the renovation is completed, temporarily borrow the office of the Overseas Chinese General Association. (d) Set up a refugee shelter in the preparatory office first, and decide to set up a start-up fund of 4,000 yuan, asking the Overseas Chinese General Association to allocate 2,000 yuan from the refugee relief fund, and asking the Guangzhao Association to allocate 2,000 yuan. (e) Temporarily set the operating expenses of the maintenance association at 500 yuan per month, which will be raised by the maintenance association or the preparatory office. (f) Hire lawyer Wu Chengyu as a legal advisor. (g) Hire Comrade Peng Canguang as an advisor. It was resolved to stipulate the following measures: (a) Temporarily set the Overseas Chinese Factory Fund at 600,000 yuan, and ask the Overseas Chinese General Association to be responsible for raising 200,000 yuan, ask all sectors of Shanghai and various charitable organizations to be responsible for raising 200,000 yuan, and the Refugee Relief Association to find ways to raise 200,000 yuan. (b) Hire Xu Shiying, Guo Shun, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Wang Yiting, Zheng Hongnian, Shi Dezhi, Jian Yujie, Huang Jinrong, Tang Haian, Wu Chengyu, Peng Canguang, and Huang Zhulin as 13 members of the Fund Custody Committee to organize the Fund Custody Committee, and appoint Xu Shiying as the chairman and Guo Shun as the vice chairman. (c) Chiang Chairman's donation of 10,000 yuan will be used as the Overseas Chinese Factory Fund, and after receiving it, it will be submitted to the aforementioned Custody Committee for safekeeping in order to show seriousness, and will still be stored in the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Bank. (d) The preparatory work for the Overseas Chinese Factory will be handed over to the Refugee Relief Association to formulate a plan for separate discussions in the future. (e) Sincerely invite Mayor Wu Tiecheng to be the General Supervisor of the establishment of the Overseas Chinese Factory. (3) Representative Lin Wenli proposed to hold a banquet for the press and all sectors of Shanghai to report on the truth of the anti-Chinese incidents in Mexico, please submit the proposal for discussion and resolution. It was resolved to hold a banquet at the Xinxin Restaurant at 7 PM on the 24th of this month.

I urge you to dispel suspicions and cease fighting immediately. Even if you win in fratricidal strife, it is not glorious. The loss of the country and the destruction of the nation are imminent. I send this telegram in detail and hope for your clear instruction." In addition to telegraphing to the central government, I hereby inform you. Liu Xiang bows respectfully.

The Trial Period for the Cotton Mill Production Cuts Has Ended 125

With No Improvement, Each Factory Will Decide Its Own Measures

The Central News Agency reports that the National Cotton Mill Association decided to cut production by 23 percent, starting on the 22nd of last month, for a one-month trial period to regulate the production and sales of cotton yarn. After the implementation, there was no improvement. Therefore, on the 10th of this month, a second discussion was held. Everyone believed that the low price of yarn and the lack of sales led to the accumulation of goods and economic difficulties, which could not be solved by production cuts. Moreover, the proposed assistance measures after submitting a request to the government are not a fundamental solution. As the situation of each factory is different, no further decisions can be made to force each factory to implement it uniformly. It was decided that after the one-month trial period expires, each factory will consider its own situation and decide on measures. Yesterday was the last day of the trial period. The reporter specially went to the Cotton Mill Association to inquire. According to its person in charge, it is not yet known whether each factory will continue to implement production cuts after the expiration or will restore the original state, or even shut down completely. As the situation of each factory is different, each factory will implement its own measures arbitrarily, making it difficult to obtain accurate statistics. In short, the situation has not been alleviated, and those who restore the original state will be limited to a few factories with relatively strong financial resources. As for the impact of the increase in tariffs on Japanese yarn after the expiration of the Sino-Japanese tariff agreement, it is not significant. There are many Japanese factories in China, centered on Shanghai, and their sales channels are in the Yellow River basin and the northern provinces, where Chinese yarn is almost extinct. The impact of competition is not small. Therefore, Japanese businessmen are very optimistic about the yarn industry, and pay special attention to the production and sales of fine yarn, while Chinese businessmen are in a precarious situation. If the government does not have fundamental measures, and the people do not make efforts to promote it, the serious situation cannot be reduced.

Land Bureau Opens Measurement of Yinhang District Households 129

Four Items to Note

The Shanghai Land Bureau, in order to measure the household lands of the twenty-third bao, second and fifteenth tu of Yinhang District, and to inform all property owners to go to fill out forms and receive measurements, has issued a special announcement, saying: For the matter of the announcement, the bureau is now starting to measure the household lands of the twenty-third bao, second and fifteenth tu of Yinhang District. All property owners should pay attention to the following items: (1) The local保 (baos) will distribute filling forms to the property owners. Each property owner should, within ten days after receiving the form, truthfully fill it out and return it to the local 保 (bao) to collect and submit to the second measurement team of the bureau at 70 Tongjia Road, or the property owner can directly submit it to the measurement team. (2) If a property owner's address is unknown, resulting in the filling form not being distributed and not received, they can directly fill out the form at the bureau or the second measurement team. (3) If a property owner's land deed is pledged out, making it impossible to fill in the name of the household and the mu (畝) acreage of the land, they should immediately copy it from the pledgee and not shirk responsibility. (4) When each household's land is measured, the property owner must, together with the local 保 (bao), clearly point out the boundaries in all four directions to the investigators and measurers, or entrust a representative to point out the boundaries on the spot in advance. Otherwise, the bureau will only rely on the instructions of the local 保 (bao). If any errors or disputes arise in the future, the property owner will be responsible. The above four items are all related to the consolidation of property rights. In addition to instructing the local 保 (baos) of the said tu to comply, it is imperative to announce it to all so that each property owner pays special attention to it. This announcement.

China National Aviation Corporation Regularly Holds Board Meetings 130

According to the Central News Agency, the China National Aviation Corporation is scheduled to hold its nineteenth board meeting at 9:30 am next Monday (the 22nd), at which it will report and decide on opening routes to Chongqing, Chengdu, Shanghai, and Guangzhou. The details are explored and recorded as follows:

Board Meeting The nineteenth board meeting is scheduled to be held at 9 am on the 22nd. Notices have been issued. Most of the Chinese and American directors are in Shanghai and can attend. It is not yet known whether Zhu Jia-hua, Minister of Communications, and Shen Shu-hua, Director-General of General Affairs, will come to Shanghai to attend. The meeting will discuss various internal affairs, and the preparations for the trial flights of the Shanghai-Guangzhou route will be submitted for approval. However, the opening and establishment costs of the Shanghai-Guangzhou line will be approximately one million yuan. Therefore, whether the unpaid capital will be continued to be paid by China and the United States will also be discussed.

Shanghai-Beiping Line Recently, Tianjin and Beiping have been very panicked. The Shanghai-Beiping air route is one of the important transportation routes. According to the person in charge of the company, the line will not be suspended unless absolutely necessary. The head of the flight department has been sent to Beiping next Tuesday to preside over the matter. Mr. Bandi will return to Shanghai next week to report.

Shanghai-Guangzhou Line The Shanghai-Guangzhou line is expected to begin trial flights in early July. Offices are being established in various ports in Zhejiang, Fujian, and Guangdong provinces, and radio stations are being installed. However, due to the prosperity of commerce and the high land prices in various ports, a large amount of land is needed. Therefore, floating pontoons, ferry boats, and docks needed for landing on the sea are being actively prepared. Moreover, since the Shanghai-Guangzhou line is longer and there are many merchants and travelers, two twin-engine amphibious aircraft will be ordered. They have very high speeds and can arrive on the same day, carrying more than a dozen passengers and a large amount of mail. The price of each aircraft is approximately 180,000 to 190,000 yuan. Once the line is officially opened, the aircraft can be used for direct flights between the two places.

Chengdu The new Chengdu aircraft is scheduled to make its maiden flight next Tuesday from Shanghai to Hankou and will be deployed on that line in the future.

Misunderstanding Regarding Ding Muhuan's Name 131

A previous report stated that Ding Muhuan held an official position in the puppet state. It has been found that this is Ding Muhuan from Fengtian, not Ding Muhuan from Wuxi, the former director of the Aviation Administration. Recently, rumors have spread that Mr. Ding's house has been sealed. This is completely inaccurate. According to Mr. Ding Fubao, he recently inquired about this matter with General Zhu Ziqiao. General Zhu said that he often met with Mr. Ding Muhuan from Wuxi in Beiping recently. The person holding an official position in the puppet state is actually someone else. The rumors circulating outside are mostly misunderstandings, and there is no such thing as a house being sealed.

丨Kong Xiangxi and Others Elected as Committee Members丨

Silk Cocoon Factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Open One After Another 133

Cocoon Price Approximately 25 to 35 Cents Per Catty

Silk merchants in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, as spring cocoons are about to be on the market in various places, are following the annual practice of suspending work to organize cocoon collection in various places. Shaoxing in Zhejiang province first opened the market, with a price of 28 cents per catty. Jiaxing opened on the 19th, and Pingyao opened yesterday, with a price of 31 cents per catty. Chang'an will open on the 22nd. Generally, the cocoon price ranges from 25 to 35 cents. Wuxi, Liyang, and other places in Jiangsu province will be on the market as late as the end of this month or early June. The number of cocoon merchants and the amount of spring cocoon production in various places have increased compared to last year. Silver shops are providing as much credit as possible to silk cocoon merchants with good credit. More than 50 silk factories in the city are expected to start work after the new cocoons are on the market.

Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau Revises Regulations on Resident's Lease Guarantee 137

To be Implemented from June 1st

The Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau has been handling the interim measures for housing guarantees based on Article 5 of the Regulations for Punishing Kidnappers. Now that the regulations have been ordered to be canceled, the previous measures and guarantees are no longer applicable. However, in order to eliminate bandits and protect public security, it should continue to be handled. Therefore, the bureau revised the measures and guarantees and changed them to the "Shanghai Municipal Resident Guarantee Measures" and submitted them to the municipal government and the Executive Yuan for approval. The bureau has now decided to uniformly use the new guarantees from June 1st of this year and ordered the departments to handle them on schedule and announced them to the citizens. The bureau's revised resident guarantee measures are copied as follows: "Article 1. In order to eliminate bandits and maintain public security in this city, all residents of this city must seek proper guarantees in accordance with the provisions of these measures. Article 2. The resident guarantee measures are as follows: (1) Store guarantee (those who have opened a store in this city for more than one year); (2) Resident guarantee (those who have lived in this city for more than one year and have a proper occupation); (3) Those who reside in self-owned houses should present the deed or be certified by the village chief to be exempted from the guarantee, but those who wish to handle it in accordance with items 1 and 2 may do so; (4) Slum dwellers and earthen houses should provide a joint guarantee of five neighboring households; (5) Foreigners without guarantees may be certified by the consular office, and those from countries without treaties may be guaranteed by a foreigner registered with the bureau; (6) Party members and civil servants may be certified by the competent authority and exempted from the guarantee. Article 3. The responsibility of the guarantor in the preceding paragraph is limited to harboring bandits and disturbing public security. Article 4. When landlords and tenants lease houses or sub-renters (i.e., second landlords and third landlords) sublet houses, regardless of shops or residences, they shall comply with the provisions of Article 2 and instruct the tenants to seek guarantees separately or have the landlord and sub-renters fill out the guarantee and submit it to the competent district office for filing. Article 5. If the guarantor changes his residence or closes his business after providing the guarantee, the guaranteed person shall declare it to the competent district office and seek another proper guarantee. Article 6. If the guarantor does not wish to guarantee the guaranteed person, he may declare it to the competent district office, and the competent district office shall promptly order the guaranteed person to seek another proper guarantee. Article 7. The competent district office shall immediately check the guarantee when it is received. If it is not accurate, the competent district office shall promptly order it to be replaced and re-checked every six months thereafter. Article 8. Landlords or sub-renters and sub-letters who do not comply with these measures may be punished in accordance with Article 34 of the Police Violation Law and still be ordered to seek a guarantee. If they still fail to provide a guarantee within the time limit, the competent district office may submit it to the bureau for verification. Article 9. If there are any matters not covered by these measures, they may be submitted for revision. Article 10. These measures shall be implemented from the date of approval by the municipal government."

Tian Huan Returns to Shanghai to Sell Books in His Spare Time 141

Tian Huan, compiler of the Central Party History and advisor to the General Headquarters for the Suppression of Bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, is also a famous calligrapher and painter in recent times. He once sold his books in Shanghai, and those who obtained his paintings and writings treasured them as priceless gems. He was famous throughout the country. In the winter of the twelfth year of the Republic of China, President Sun telegraphed him to go to Guangdong for revolutionary affairs. After that, he traveled north and south as an official, and had no time for this. The flood in Hubei two years ago was extremely severe. He Chengbing, chairman of the province, organized a flood relief committee and hired him as a committee member stationed in Shanghai, requesting him to launch a national calligraphy and painting relief effort and requesting him to sell his books for one month. All the proceeds were used for flood relief. At that time, those who admired Tian's calligraphy and painting eagerly requested them, and there was a situation where he could not handle them all. Before long, he obtained a large sum of money and handed it over to the association as agreed. It is a pity that the time limit was too short, and those who cherished Tian's calligraphy lamented. This time he returned to Shanghai and plans to sell his books in his spare time. The price list is being rushed to be printed and will be published in various newspapers after it is printed. It is heard that the receiving address is 72 Yongyu Lane, Beile Road, French Concession, and major stationery and fan shops in the city.

Woman from Tangkou Dies Tragically Under Wheels 142

Qian Zhou, a woman from Tangkou, also known as Zhou Chen, 38 years old, worked as a servant at 4 Tai'an Lane, Beile Road, French Concession. At 9:15 am on the 19th, she went out and returned home, crossing the road from north to south at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Beile Road. A car number 8330, driven by a Westerner, was driving from east to west. In order to avoid Zhou, the front of the car turned to the left, causing it to hit the water gate on the side of the road. Unexpectedly, the rear of the car hit Zhou, causing head injuries. She was taken to the Guangren Hospital by the police. She died of her injuries shortly after arriving at the hospital. The hospital notified the police, who took the body to the morgue of the Tongren Fuyuan branch. Yesterday, Deng, the prosecutor of the Second Special District Court, arrived at the morgue upon request of the Vehicle Affairs Office and determined that the deceased had died from injuries caused by being hit by a car. He ordered the body to be handed over to Hua Gendi, the deceased's cousin, for burial. Whether the defendant was at fault will be handled by the Vehicle Affairs Office.

Norwegian Ship Sinks He'an Wheel in Collision 145

Crew and Passengers Fortunately All Safe

Loss of Approximately 250,000 Yuan

The He'an Wheel of the He'ai Wheel Company of Wai Xiang Gua Street in Nanshi, which set sail from Shanghai to Amoy yesterday morning, collided with the Johanne Justesen (transliteration) of the Norwegian merchant Da Feng Company while passing near Gaoqiao at about 9 o'clock. The He'an Wheel immediately sank. The details are recorded below:

Circumstances of the Collision 146

The He'an Wheel loaded a large amount of grain and passengers at floating pontoon numbers 6 and 7 at Nan Wharf at 7:30 yesterday morning and set sail for Sandu, Amoy. At 9:40, while passing through location number 4 and 5 near Gaoqiao, it encountered a Norwegian ship of the Da Feng Company entering from Wusong, which did not follow the shipping lane and sailed straight. According to the Huangpu River shipping lane, outgoing ships should sail on the left side of the Huangpu River, and incoming ships should sail on the right side (that is, the west side of the Huangpu River). The He'an Wheel saw the Norwegian ship sailing into the same shipping lane and being very close, fearing the danger of a collision, so it urgently sounded the horn. The Norwegian ship also sounded the horn, but did not move to avoid the He'an Wheel then turned towards Pudong. Because it was close to the shoals, it was unable to accelerate, so it had to slightly turn the bow of the ship in the hope of avoiding danger.

He'an Sunk in Collision 147

One side urgently sounded the horn, while at the same time quickly turned the ship, but the Norwegian ship, for some reason, continued to rush straight down, so it was unable to avoid the collision. The He'an Wheel was hit with great force below the waterline of the stern, and river water poured into the cabin. The shipowner, upon learning of the collision, rushed to Pudong Shoal, but the entire ship sank to the bottom of the river in less than five minutes. After causing the accident, the Norwegian ship continued to sail to Shanghai.

Rescue Status 148

When the He'an was sunk in the collision, a customs river patrol vessel happened to pass by and sailed close to the ship for rescue. A small Asia Petroleum Storage vessel nearby heard the plea for help and also rushed to the side of the ship to assist the customs vessel in the rescue. Therefore, the crew and passengers were completely rescued without any injuries. After the He'an Wheel had an accident, the crew and passengers were rescued with the help of customs and Asia Petroleum Storage vessels. The shipowner then reported to the customs and sent the river management department to inspect the scene of the accident. After learning of the accident, the shipping administration bureau also sent personnel to inspect.

Company Negotiations 149

Hetae Company only received the report of the He'an Wheel being sunk by the Da Feng Norwegian Wheel at noon yesterday. It immediately sent a letter to negotiate, but because yesterday was Saturday, the company stopped working in the afternoon, so there was no reply until the evening. As a result, the goods in the ship could not be salvaged. Today is also Sunday, so it will be necessary for both parties to send personnel to jointly inspect tomorrow before salvage can begin.

Heavy Losses 150

The wheel weighs 1,100 tons. This time, it was sailing from Shanghai to Sandu, Amoy. In addition to carrying 38 passengers, the ship contained a large amount of grain, including more than 6,000 bags of indica rice, 12,000 bags of flour, about 1,500 bags of soybeans, and local cloth and miscellaneous goods, worth about 150,000 yuan. The ship price was also more than 90,000 yuan. The total loss this time is about 250,000 yuan. After the passengers were rescued and returned to Shanghai, the company immediately refunded their tickets. The sinking location of the wheel obstructs the shipping lane, so it is urgent to find a way to salvage it. However, before the two parties have inspected it, it is not convenient to move it because it is related to future negotiations. At high tide, only the flagpole and chimney of the wheel can be seen. At low tide, the river bank is also exposed on the surface of the water.

Yu Yongkang Sues Stepmother to Confirm Status as Adopted Son 151

Raised and Married Off by Adoptive Father

With Witnesses Available from that Time to Testify

| Debate Concluded, Judgment Scheduled for the 25th |

Yu Ying, a woman from Ningbo, Yin County, residing at No. 18, Huayan Lane, Maite Hesitu Road, is already in her fifties. Her husband, Yu Caixing, formerly the head foreman in the weaving room of the Sanxin Yarn Factory, passed away last winter, leaving behind a million in assets, all controlled by Mrs. Yu. However, Yu Caixing had previously adopted Yongkang, the son of his elder brother Dingfu, as his heir, raised him to adulthood, and even arranged his marriage. Unexpectedly, Yu Ying now suddenly denies Yongkang's status as an adopted son. Yongkang, in order to preserve his rightful name and rights, has filed a lawsuit against his stepmother in the First Special District Court. Initially, he requested mediation, but when that failed, he formally filed a lawsuit. His complaint states that when the plaintiff was eight years old, Caixing, having no children of his own, obtained the consent of his biological father, Dingfu, to adopt the plaintiff as his heir. He was immediately taken in and raised to adulthood, and Caixing even arranged his marriage, acting as the officiant. All of this can be proven by witnesses from that time. Dingfu was previously the head foreman in the weaving room of the Sanxin Yarn Factory, and was diligent and cautious in his work, highly valued by the factory's chief engineer. Later, when the chief engineer returned to his home country, he gave Dingfu a letter of recommendation. After Dingfu's death, his adoptive father, Caixing, used the letter to take his place, claiming that they had the same work experience, and was thus able to become the head foreman, accumulating a great deal of wealth over more than twenty years. Last year, the adoptive father passed away, and all the property is now managed by the defendant. The plaintiff has legally asserted his rights, but the defendant has ignored the facts and denied the plaintiff's status as Caixing's heir. However, the plaintiff's adoption is clearly evidenced, and is well known to relatives and friends. The facts are clear, and cannot be arbitrarily denied. Therefore, he respectfully requests that the court swiftly summon witnesses and render a judgment confirming the plaintiff's status as Yu Caixing's heir, so as to ensure the proper ancestral rites, etc. After being sued, Yu Ying also hired a lawyer to file a defense. Li Hu, the presiding judge of the civil court of the First Special District Court, held a hearing on May 13th, summoning both the plaintiff and defendant, as well as witnesses, for examination. According to Yu Yongkang's testimony, "My biological father died when I was nine years old. My wife was chosen for me by my adoptive father. The matchmaker is still alive and can testify." The defendant, Yu Ying, consistently denied the adoption. All witnesses from both sides were questioned one by one. Yesterday morning, the court continued to question the witnesses, and then the plaintiff's lawyer, Wang Peiyuan, and the defendant's representative, Lawyer Huang, concluded their arguments. Judge Li announced that the judgment would be pronounced on the 25th of this month.

Robbery and Murder of Township Head's Family in Chenjia Baizhang, Dachang, Three Lives Lost 153

One Thousand Yuan in Cash, Silver, and Clothing Stolen

Two Rifles and Seven Hundred Rounds of Ammunition Taken

A robbery occurred around 11 PM the night before last in Chenjia Baizhang, about six hundred yards southwest of Dachang Town in Baoshan County. The township head and his wife were both shot and killed. The wife was also pregnant and about to give birth. Two rifles and seven hundred rounds of ammunition used by the defense corps were also stolen. Details are listed below:

Village Survey 154

Chenjia Baizhang Village is located about six li southwest of Dachang Town in Baoshan County, close to Zhenru. It faces south and backs north, with about fifty households. To the east is a small bridge, a winding dirt road leading to Dachang Town. There are no villages nearby around the village. Most of the villagers live by farming, with spinning and weaving as secondary occupations.

Details of the Robbery 155

Around 11 PM the night before last, during a heavy downpour with thunder and lightning, more than ten robbers speaking with a Jiangsu-Zhejiang accent suddenly arrived, each armed with pistols, Mauser pistols, rifles, and so on. They swarmed into the home of Chen Mingguang, the township head and first platoon leader of the ninth Jia of the defense corps. Chen had already gone to bed, but the gate was not locked. Chen had two younger brothers who, although they lived separately, still resided in the same house, which had three courtyards. Chen lived in the back courtyard. When the robbers entered, they took temporary shelter in the gatehouse due to the heavy rain. There was a bicycle parked in the gatehouse, and one of the robbers started playing with the bicycle wheel, which Chen heard. Chen immediately got up and shouted, but the robbers took the opportunity to rush in, drag Chen to the courtyard entrance, and shoot him several times with a Mauser pistol, killing him. His wife, Zhang, hearing her husband's silence, ran out of bed. However, she was shot in the abdomen with a pistol at the entrance to the main room, also killing her. Seeing that Chen and his wife were both dead, the robbers then went to search the bedrooms.

Investigation of Losses 156

A total of fifty yuan in cash and silver were taken from the deceased's body. From the deceased's room, a gold ring, a pair of gold earrings, two silk-faced leather coats, two silk-lined jackets, and a silk skirt were stolen. Robbing the room of the deceased's eldest son, the robbers learned that Chen was the platoon leader of the defense corps, so they first ordered his son to hand over the firearms. The son, named Hexin, could not resist and had to give the firearms to the robbers. These included a Type 38 rifle with 500 rounds of ammunition, and a Russian rifle with 200 rounds of ammunition, as well as two silk-faced leather robes, two pairs of silk trousers, and two long gowns. From Hexin's wife, Zhou (newly married last year), two silk qipaos, a cotton-padded jacket, and one silk-lined jacket and trousers, seven foreign cloth qipaos, and five lined jackets and trousers were taken. Also, one leather robe and one leather vest belonging to the deceased were taken, with a total value of over one thousand yuan.

Deceased's Family 157

The deceased had two younger brothers, Chen Xiannian, 32 years old, and Chen Youxian, 28 years old. There was also an elderly mother, Mrs. Yang, 58 years old, four sons, and a daughter-in-law. The eldest son, Hexin, is 19 years old, and the daughter-in-law, Zhou, is 20 years old. The second son, Fuxin, is 13 years old, the third son, Wenxin, is 9 years old, and the fourth son, Rongxin, is 3 years old. There is also a daughter named Yuejin, 6 years old.

Deceased's Wounds 158

Yesterday afternoon at around 1 PM, after the reporter arrived at the scene and learned of the above situation, Hexin led him to the main room to inspect the wounds of the deceased. Chen Mingxian was lying face up on the boards in the middle of the main room, wearing a white cloth short shirt and white and blue striped cloth pants, barefoot. There was a gunshot wound in the middle of his left chest, above the nipple, and another gunshot wound an inch below his left shoulder. Mrs. Zhang was lying next to the west wall, her abdomen swollen, as if she was about to give birth, wearing a black cloth short shirt, blue cloth pants, and black socks. There was a gunshot wound an inch above her navel, but the bullets did not pass through. The deceased's son, Hexin, has reported the incident to the Dachang Town Public Security Bureau, which has forwarded it to the Baoshan County Government for investigation. According to Hexin, the robbers also instructed him not to make any noise when they left, otherwise they would come back and shoot him. They fired more than ten shots from their rifles along the way as they left.

Cash and Silver Preserved, but Life Not 159

Robber Angrily Fires a Shot

Gong Chunshui Dies Loyal to His Employer

Kong Xinyi, a Ningbo native residing at No. 4, Bao'an Fang, Nanyang Bridge, Biel Road, French Concession, is 38 years old and runs a lace export business, setting up the Xinji Lace Shop in his residence. He employs Gong Chunshui (54 years old this year), a native of Nanxiang, as a clerk, with a monthly salary of fourteen yuan, specializing in collecting and distributing lace in the countryside of Changshu. Gong has been in this position for three years and is loyal to his duties, greatly valued by his employer. Gong usually takes the raw materials from Shanghai to the countryside to be made by female workers. When a batch is finished, Gong brings the goods back to Shanghai, settles the wages, and takes the money back to the countryside to pay the workers. This time, Gong brought goods to Shanghai from Changshu before the 20th and stayed at the home of his employer, Kong Xinyi, at No. 4, Bao'an Fang, Biel Road. The night before last, Kong settled the accounts for a total of four hundred yuan and gave the cash to Gong, preparing to go to the countryside yesterday morning. Yesterday morning at 4:30 AM, Gong left Kong's residence, put the money in his pocket, and went out the back door to hire a rickshaw to the North Railway Station to catch the first train to Kunshan and then to Changshu. Unexpectedly, just two or three steps out of the back door, as he was hailing a rickshaw, a robber of medium build, wearing a blue cloth shirt and trousers, a copper basin hat, and rubber overshoes, suddenly emerged from the alley and stopped Gong, trying to rob the money in Gong's pocket. At that moment, Gong grabbed the robber with one hand and pressed down on his pocket with the other, backing away while shouting, "You (referring to the Kong family), come out quickly!" As he struggled with the robber, he backed up to the Kong family's back door. At this time, Xu Hu, a 36-year-old maid from Changshu in the Kong family, had just gotten up and was going outside the back door to wash a chamber pot. She saw Gong grappling with someone and mistakenly thought it was a fight, so she stepped forward to mediate. Gong was then able to break free and flee towards the back door. Just as one foot crossed the threshold of the back door, the robber, hating the maid for interfering and causing him to fail in his purpose, drew a handgun and fired a shot at the woman and Gong. The bullet hit Gong in the right waist, piercing his left waist, and he fell to the ground, blood gushing out. The robber immediately turned and fled without a trace. When the employer, Kong Xinyi, was awakened from his sleep, he got up and went downstairs. He saw Gong lying in the kitchen, unable to speak, bleeding profusely. He quickly hired a car to take Gong to Renji Hospital for treatment and reported the incident to the police to apprehend the robber. Detectives went to the scene of the incident to investigate and recovered a bullet casing, which they took back to the police station for verification. However, Gong's injury was in a vital area, and he died before he could be treated. The hospital notified the police, who sent detectives to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-Hall for an autopsy, and summoned Gong Xueli (26 years old, working at the Zhabei Second Section Fire Brigade), Gong's son, and the witness Xu Hu to the station. At 10 AM, the police reported to the Second Special District Court, which appointed Prosecutor Deng Baosun and forensic doctor to the scene to examine the body. The detectives reported the previous situation and presented the stolen money. The deceased's son requested that the robber be apprehended and justice be served. The maid Xu Hu testified about the circumstances of the deceased's struggle with the robber and being shot down. The official ruled that Gong Chunshui's death was indeed caused by a gunshot wound. The body was handed over to the family for burial, and the police department was ordered to apprehend the murderer and bring him to justice.

A Visit to the First Special District Women's Prison Amidst Calls for Prison Reform 160

Zhang Wenqing, Who Murdered Her Stepmother, is Skilled in Embroidery

The Female Inmates Are Mostly Between Thirty and Forty Years Old

| Most Cases Involve Opium Offenses |

Since Mr. Dong Shoujing, a prominent figure in the French Concession, submitted a petition to the Ministry of Judicial Administration on behalf of the prisoners in the Caohejing Prison, a movement to improve prison treatment has swept through the city. Besides Caohejing, there are several other prisons within the special districts, but the situation inside them is not well understood by outsiders. Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, the reporter took a car to the First Special District Women's Prison to inspect the conditions inside. The warden, Sun Xiong, personally received us, and after a pleasant conversation, guided us through the entire facility. We found that all the equipment was well-organized, and the management, education, and sanitation of the prisoners were particularly well done. Warden Sun, whose courtesy name is Yongmou, is from Hunan and is skilled in prison management. Since taking office, he has made great efforts to reorganize the prison, leading to today's achievements. The prison was originally reorganized from the women's detention center of the former Mixed Court. It is now called the Jiangsu Second Prison Branch and is located to the right of the Jiangsu Higher Court Second Branch. The building has four floors. Currently, the first floor houses the warden's office, staff offices, the doctor's office, the education office, and the prisoners' bathroom and laundry room. The remaining eight rooms are used as detention rooms for criminal defendants awaiting trial. The second floor has eight rooms each for the prisoners' infirmary and opium detoxification room. The third and fourth floors are entirely used as prison cells. The cells on the fourth floor are named "Propriety" and "Righteousness," and those on the third floor are named "Integrity" and "Shame." Each section has four rooms, and each room used to hold seven people, so the entire prison could only hold a hundred or so people. In recent years, the number of crimes has increased, and the number of criminals has also increased. Currently, the prison holds more than 400 people, almost three times the designated capacity. The rooms are inevitably crowded. With the arrival of summer, Warden Sun pays great attention to the prisoners' hygiene, requiring the resident doctor to make rounds for examinations every day, and the prison guards work hard to keep the place clean. A special supply department has also been set up, so if a sick prisoner wants food beyond the prescribed menu, it will be provided by the supply department with the prison doctor's permission. Ordinary food is provided three times a day, with two dry meals and one wet meal. The prisoners currently work at sewing clothes, weaving towels, and embroidery. However, there are only two people who are skilled in embroidery, one of whom is Zhang Wenqing, the protagonist of the sensational case of murdering her stepmother that occurred some years ago. In addition to doing manual labor, the prisoners must take courses on elementary literacy and the Three Principles of the People for a certain amount of time each morning, and do freehand exercises for half an hour each afternoon. According to Warden Sun, the female prisoners in the entire prison are mostly between the ages of thirty and forty. Most of the cases involve opium offenses, accounting for about 40%. The remaining cases, such as disturbing public morals and theft, account for about 10% to 15% or 20%. Although the number of prisoners is increasing every day, the food allowance remains the same as the designated quota for one hundred and several dozen people, making it quite difficult to manage the budget.

Policeman Beats a Man to Death 161

Shen Bingwen's Refusal to Accept Mediation Was Certainly Wrong

The Policeman on Patrol Who Beat a Man to Death Should be Severely Punished

Shen Bingwen, a 63-year-old man from Jiading who was employed at the Xu Family Garden in Nansheng, District 9, Sanmin Road, Zhenru, has been working for decades and has no family. According to his cohabitant, he had a conflict with a neighboring woman over trivial matters the afternoon before last, and the noise was heard outside. A patrolman from the Third Precinct of the Fourth District happened to pass by and entered to investigate and mediate. Unexpectedly, Shen refused to accept the mediation and responded with abusive language, causing the policeman to become enraged. The policeman then struck Shen's chest with the butt of his pistol, followed by punches and kicks, beating Shen Bingwen to death on the spot. Seeing that he had caused a disaster, the policeman tried to escape, but was detained by the precinct chief, Yao Chongnai, who ordered a patrol officer to guard him. Yesterday, he ordered the local bailiff, Li Yuxiang, to report the death to the District Court for inspection. However, the bailiff confusedly reported that Shen Bingwen had died, had no family, and that was the extent of the report. Prosecutor Kong Xianglin and Coroner Xuan Zhiming were appointed and went to Zhenru for inspection. After hearing reports from the cohabitant and others, the official inspected the deceased's body and found multiple wounds, and the sixth rib had been broken by the beating. It was determined that the death was caused by injuries sustained during his lifetime. An autopsy report was completed, and the body was ordered to be collected. The bailiff was severely reprimanded and ordered to bring witnesses to the court for questioning the next day. The precinct was ordered to send the patrolman to the Public Security Bureau for investigation and punishment. The Third Precinct of the Fourth District has now submitted the patrolman to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Repays Old Debts to Various Households 162

Payment Made in Five Categories

Since the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was nationalized, the board of directors established a Debt Consolidation Committee to handle various debts. Yesterday morning at 10 AM, various creditors, such as Ruichangxiang and Senchang coal companies, as well as various hardware, construction, and machinery companies and factories, petitioned the board of directors again, requesting continued repayment. General Manager Liu Hongsheng received them and agreed to follow the previous board of directors' resolution: debts over 100,000 yuan would be repaid by another 10%, debts between 10,000 and 100,000 yuan would be repaid by 15%, debts between 1,000 and 10,000 yuan would be repaid by 20%, debts under 1,000 yuan would be repaid in two installments, and debts under 500 yuan would be repaid in full. The accounting department was notified to make the payments. The creditors began receiving payments from the accounting department at 10 AM.

Mr. Huang Renzhi's Speech on National Humiliation Week: My Views on the Future of Sino-Japanese Relations 171

Ladies and gentlemen, I received that notice from the YMCA a few days ago, and it really presented me with a difficult problem. Because many gentlemen have spoken about this topic several times already, and this time I am speaking as the last one. You must know that it's not easy to speak last, because almost everything I want to say has already been said by the previous speakers. It just so happens that I am at the rear, which is really my unfortunate fate. Moreover, I just suffered a little loss, because Mr. Wang Yunwu originally wanted to push me to speak first. At that time, I thought I would just be polite for a moment, and if he insisted again, I could take advantage of speaking first. Unexpectedly, he didn't decline any further. So everything I wanted to say was already said by him. That's really a big loss.

However, this topic is about my views, and not your views or his views. Thinking about it, my views must be my personal opinions, different from other people's opinions. Now, I'll first divide it into two sides, as the saying goes, "Know yourself and know your enemy." First, let's look at the Japanese side. I didn't pay much attention to it before. Although I have been in social service for thirty years and have been to Japan four times, I only inspected education and didn't really look at its politics, economy, and other aspects. Until the spring of the year before last, when I went to Japan, I unexpectedly received a great shock. Because I suddenly saw that the general situation was one of high spirits and great excitement. The people were all talking about how to attack the Soviet Union, how to attack the United States, and how to first plunder our Northeast and conquer China. It really seemed like a surging tide. However, when I heard it at that time, I just thought they were saying it like our Chinese people shouting about "Down with Imperialism." So I didn't pay much attention to it. Before the September 18th Incident, I wrote a book called "A Voyage Around the Yellow Sea." Who would have thought that we had just forgotten about it, and soon the September 18th Incident happened. At that time, I deeply blamed myself for being useless and rebuked myself for being muddleheaded. Since I knew the above situation in Japan, I should have returned and used twenty-four percent sincerity, or even tearfully pleaded with the authorities, urging everyone to pay attention. I shouldn't have regarded it as just empty talk. But I didn't expect that such a great disaster would befall us. Since the September 18th Incident, there was the January 28th Incident that Mr. Wang Yunwu just talked about. Not long after, it continued. And it wasn't just the January 28th Incident, there was also Shanhaiguan, Nantianmen, Rehe, Luanhe, and so on. So their words were definitely not empty talk, but really something they did.

Let's not talk about Japan for now. Let's talk about China. But some people ask me, saying what will China be like in the future? I reply to them, "Whatever you want it to be, it will be." This is not a joke. I can give a few examples. The September 18th Incident, although it was Japan's premeditated plan, was also because Zhang Xueliang and a group of Northeast officials wanted it to be that way. It wasn't just that Zhang Xueliang and others' non-resistance was what they wanted, but also that the people of the three northeastern provinces wanted it to be that way. Let's talk about Rehe. I have been to Rehe, but it hadn't been lost when I went. Not long after I returned, Rehe was lost. But do you all know how Rehe was lost? It wasn't because Japanese soldiers came and drove Tang Yulin away. We know that Tang Yulin was the chairman of Rehe. He usually not only didn't pay attention to the people's livelihood and suffering, but also exploited the people, forcing them to grow opium and openly manufacturing morphine. This made the people suffer unspeakably. Even when the enemy came, they were unwilling to cooperate with Tang Yulin. So the Japanese army was able to seize Rehe so effortlessly because Tang Yulin didn't want Rehe. If he loved Rehe, he wouldn't have engaged in such rampant extortion. There were also several generals such as Zhang Zuoxiang who were initially unwilling to go, and only went when the crisis was imminent. Of course, it was too late. In fact, it was because everyone didn't want Rehe, so Rehe was given away for others to take. All of the above past facts show that whatever you want it to be, it will be. So predicting the future, it will also be whatever you want it to be. But my hope is that it won't be anything.

What I want to contribute today is that there are several mentalities that must not be had. If you have these mentalities, it will definitely be whatever you don't want it to be. I have a friend whose son is studying at school. One day, he went back to see his father and said to his father, "There's no hope for China. It's better to let it perish." His father blamed him for saying such a thing, but he retorted, "Dad, you don't know. Most people in China don't have any patriotism." His father said, "You can't say that. Even if everyone is a bad person, you should still be a good person." This is a very good point. Therefore, everyone should encourage themselves and never be discouraged just because there's no hope. There are also people who say that the Chinese people haven't suffered enough. They should suffer more, and only then will there be a way out after the country is destroyed. This person's argument is certainly more insightful than my friend's son. Perhaps he has read a lot of history and seen that when the Yuan Dynasty invaded China, the Yuan Dynasty was assimilated. When the Qing Dynasty entered the pass, it was also assimilated. Our China is still China. However, we know that this is history and shouldn't compare it to the present. We must remember that in 1919, the Korean people took the opportunity of the Paris Peace Conference to seek independence. Their national spirit is truly admirable. Since the demonstration on March 2nd, the Japanese authorities' treatment of the Korean people has been one of massacre, capture, and all kinds of extremes. In one village, where there were more patriotic elements, they were even surrounded by troops and massacred. As a result, in March, they killed more than 30,000 men and more than 2,000 women, and imprisoned more than 10,000. Despite such great sacrifices, independence was still not achieved. It can be seen that it is impossible to save a country after it has been destroyed. So if China wants to preserve this country, it must do so before the country is destroyed.

At the end of January this year, I went to the north and saw that Zhang Xueliang's measures were not good. Therefore, I came back and said to President Song Dai that the situation in the north is getting more and more dangerous. If the government wants this North China, it should quickly save the situation. If you have already read the evening paper today, you should know that the Japanese army has already crossed the Luan River. So if China doesn't save it now, it won't be able to save it. Now, banditry is rampant in the Yangtze River basin, disputes have occurred in Xinjiang, and Sichuan is about to have a civil war again. If this continues, China will have no place to hang this old sign. We, the people, should quickly rise up. This sign hasn't been broken yet, so we should quickly protect the sign.

Now, I have a few more words to offer to you all. First, we must strengthen our physique, just as Mr. Wang Yunwu said. In Germany, regardless of men, women, old, or young, everyone pays attention to physical fitness. Although I haven't been to Germany, I know that every household in Germany has a radio and listens to slogans and exercises every morning. We also have radios in China, but everyone just listens to ditties. The listeners here today are all outstanding people. If you go outside and see the decadent and dissolute lifestyle, it's really degenerate beyond imagination. Second, as I often say, we need science. Let's think about why we are being "tricked." It's because we don't have science. We should all work hard in the future. For example, we should teach children to study science as soon as they have knowledge. Now, I have to be rude and make a gentleman an example. Who is it? It's Mr. Wang Yunwu. He is the general manager of the Commercial Press, invented the Four-Corner Method of Character Indexing, compiled dictionaries, and can speak several languages. He is also a scientist. He studied engineering at a foreign correspondence school and obtained an engineer's diploma. After the January 28th Incident, he buried himself in hard work and managed to revive the Commercial Press in a short period of time. If the government officials could bury themselves in work like Mr. Wang, the country's situation would at least not be so bad. (End)
