Ministry of Education Stipulates University Enrollment Methods 172

▲To Avoid Talent Shortages and Surpluses

(Nanjing, 20th) The Ministry of Education believes that over the years, domestic universities and colleges have enrolled new students without limits. The proportional balance between students in liberal arts and law and students in agriculture, engineering, medicine, and science cannot be achieved, resulting in a contradictory phenomenon of talent surplus and shortage. Therefore, it has specifically stipulated the enrollment methods for universities and colleges in the 22nd year, and issued orders to all universities, colleges, and bureaus to comply with and make fundamental corrections.

China School Sports Federation Athletic Meet Closes Guanghua Affiliated Middle School Double Happiness 184

▲Field Events: Guanghua Champion, Shanghai Middle School Second, Jinan Third

▲Track Events: Guanghua Champion, Jinan Second, Fuzhong Third

Huang Feilong Sets New 200-Meter Meet Record of 23.6 Seconds

The Guanghua Affiliated Middle School track and field team, after winning the city middle school athletic meet championship, yesterday won the China School Sports Federation field event and track event championships. They scored twenty points in field events and thirty-seven points in track events. Yesterday morning it was drizzling, but fortunately it cleared up in the afternoon. However, because the field was saturated with water, the competition was inconvenient. The results were still good. Huang Feilong showed his power in the 100-meter and 200-meter races. He completed the 200-meter race in just 23.6 seconds, breaking his own meet record of 23.8 seconds, which was the most outstanding achievement of this meet. The details are as follows:

Good Sprint Results 185

▲100 meters The competition was extremely fierce. Huang Feilong, Li Songnian, Dong Yinchu, and Liu Jiayou can be called the four outstanding individuals in this event. Each of them has very even strength. Dong Yinchu, who was first in the semi-finals, fell to third place. Huang Feilong won the championship, taking only 11.6 seconds, which is quite impressive.

▲200 meters The competition for this event was as fierce as the 100-meter race. At the finish line, they were in a horizontal line, sprinting to the finish line. Jinan's Huang Feilong won the championship again, taking only 23.4 seconds, breaking his own meet record of 23.8 seconds. Guanghua's Dong Yinchu was second, Minli's Liu Jiayou was third, and Fuzhong's Cheng Zhiyuan was fourth.

Analysis of the Medal-Winning Situation 186

▲Field Events After winning the city middle school championship, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School's spirit was even more excited. However, the situation this time was quite even. In the seven events, Guanghua only won one first place, the shot put. With their even talent, they finally won the championship with twenty points. Jinan and Shanghai Middle School each won two first places. Shanghai Middle School was the runner-up with seventeen points, and Jinan was third with eleven points.

▲Track Events Guanghua's talent is the most abundant. They won a total of five first places, ranking first with thirty-seven points. Second place, Jinan Affiliated Middle School, only had fifteen points. Fudan Affiliated Middle School was one point behind in third place.

Moreover, during one of Kang Tong's jumps, I discovered her little secret: she loves small pictures. She spied the "Five Flowers" playing cards in her sister's hand and quickly hid them in her pocket, giving them a smile at the same time.

▲ Shouts from the Adjacent Field

Because the heavens were unkind, the audience in our field was sparse. However, the neighboring baseball field was filled with veterans like us making a scene, which attracted countless curious fans. It suddenly became lively. Whenever a veteran fell, there was a chorus of shouts, deafening and tantalizing.

▲ A Bouquet of Beautiful Flowers

In these times, everything is tight. Therefore, this event was not as glamorous as the Middle School Joint Association's. Only a small thatched pavilion served as the command center, and a temporary small stage served as the awards platform. The prizes were only three flags and sixty-three small medals. However, a bouquet of beautiful fresh flowers added an immeasurable amount of splendor. Unfortunately, the flowers did not end up in the hands of the athletes, but instead ended up in front of the chest of the awards presenter, Ms. Zhang Wanqing.

▲ Guanghua's Solo Act

This time, several relay races were canceled because there were no scores, so nobody wanted to run. Fortunately, the Guanghua Girls' Team performed a 200-meter race alone, otherwise, it would have been too embarrassing.

Shen Bao and Current Affairs Tie in a Heated Match 196

Each side wins one half, nothing to say.

Shi Bao beats Min Bao by two goals, content and satisfied.

Chen Bao beats Xin Wen by one, overjoyed.

▲ Three Matches Today, Starting at 3:30 PM at the Municipal Stadium

▲ (1) Shen Bao vs. Chen Bao (2) Shi Bao vs. Current Affairs (3) Min Bao vs. Xin Wen

The weather was oppressive, with lingering rain and damp ground overgrown with grass, making walking difficult. After 3:00 PM, the editorial departments of various newspapers, six teams of veterans, gradually arrived at the YMCA to gather. Because the Military Affairs Committee had issued a declaration and the Premier dared not revive old ways, the Garrison Commander simultaneously ordered the lifting of martial law. Therefore, all the athletes arrived on time. The three major battles were confusing, lacking the "intense," "enjoyable," and "thorough" experiences never seen before, no wonder the four Kang family fans are always laughing. Director Pan Gongzhan also brought his young son to watch the game, and couldn't help but smile at the exciting moments. Shen Bao's manager, Ma Yinliang, personally led a cheering squad to support and encourage the team, becoming very excited. Xin Wen Bao, Shi Chen Shi Shi Min, and other newspapers had many backstage bosses lurking around, shouting and cheering support at any time, making for a lively and exciting scene. Starting at 3:30 PM this afternoon, the six armies will rush to the public stadium and engage in another major battle.

Shi Bao Defeats Min Bao: Two to Zero

▲ Old Teng Turns into a Spotted Leopard

When Shen Huichun blew his whistle, the two Chens of Shi and Min faced each other, saying nothing. Teng Shugu passed the ball to Ren Naijing, who attacked northward. Chen Jingzhao could not block them. Lu Guangjie started from the edge and flew into the penalty area. Wu Zhongyi gritted his teeth and rushed out diagonally. Teng Shugu had outstanding martial skills and fell head over heels, dizzy and disoriented. His snow-white pants were covered in mud. He looked like a leopard from the Nan Mountain.

▲ Twelve-Yard Penalty Can Be Changed to Four Yards

But with unyielding ambition, they charged several times. Jiang Hongjiao hurriedly instructed the rear guards to strengthen their defense. Teng Wengong could not reach the State of Chu, but could only pant like a cow, sighing with emotion, "Heroes have short tempers, what can I do?" Before long, the Min Bao defender committed a twelve-yard penalty. Wang Mengnian acted as the executioner, but unexpectedly, the ball did not move, and Wang fell to the ground first. In total, the ball was about four yards away from his foot. He still angrily said to others, "If it were a four-yard penalty, I would definitely score," Those who heard this couldn't help but burst into laughter.

▲ Shi Bao Joyfully Gives Birth to Twins

In the afternoon, Shi and Min Bao's defense was in constant danger. Wu Zhongyi wielded his broadsword, killing like a demon. Hu Liangcheng even desperately ate pufferfish, falling twice in a row. Before long, Old Teng carried the ball deep, but Chen Jingzhao slipped, face-planting in the mud. Wu and Hu were outside and hadn't returned. Gao Xueguo broke out in a cold sweat, abandoning the empty goal and rushing to intercept. Just then, Old Teng had arrived. Then quickly, he fell in a double tumble. Jiang Zongdao, like a fisherman, reaped the benefits, arriving in time and kicking the ball into the net. After restarting the game, the Min Bao team was furious and launched a massive counterattack. Jiang Jianjiao constantly stirred up trouble on the east side. Li Gengxi and Cheng Changbin closed their doors, and Lei Bifeng guarded both left and right. Jiang Zongdao and Lu Guanshu supported the three southern expeditions. Old Teng was brave and skillful, venturing deep into no-man's-land. With a resounding kick, Gao Xuepu touched the ball, but it had already entered the net. He could only stare blankly, lamenting his misfortune.

▲ Chen Bao Defeats Xin Wen: One to Zero

The Chen Bao-Xin Wen match started after Shi and Min Bao. Chen Bao's goalkeeper, Hu Zongfan, had not recovered from his leg injury. He was forcibly dragged onto the field, somewhat embarrassed. He had to bear the pain, learning to be like a camel.

▲ Xin Wen Bao Misses a Good Opportunity

Amidst the sound of drums and horns, Chen Bao's Jin Xi passed the ball north. Pei Shunyuan roared, scaring the enemy back three hundred miles. The veteran Qu Yue released his horse in the eastern suburbs, with impressive momentum. Zhou Fuming remotely supported the short, fat Zi. Ma Zhishan was not good at skating, falling in a chaotic mess, even more willing to yield for the country, not kicking the ball when he saw it. This annoyed the twin-gun Lu Wenlong (Yi) and the grass-flying Shen Meizhen, who coordinated their advance. Yu Deyuan regretted being careless inside the penalty area, resulting in a twelve-yard penalty. Chen Tongsong had no strength in his foot, and the ball flew over the crossbar.

▲ Shen Meizhen's Heart is Brave Beyond Ten Thousand

Chen Bao's colleagues all clapped their hands, celebrating together towards the sky. Wang Zunwu shook his spirits. Yao Suifeng even covered her head with a white towel, looking fiercely. She peered in twice. Yu Kongwo held up his demon-revealing mirror, and the ball had nowhere to hide. Shen Meizhen glared like a bull, charging and pressing forward repeatedly. Chen Bao's defense feared her like a tiger. Yao Suifeng spread a net of iron wire, and Xu Ze spread more lime bottles. No matter how brave you are, there is no room for discussion. Wang Dexin drilled through the cracks, but suddenly rushed into Xin Wen Bao's forbidden area, facing the goal and working together. Jiang Jianhou remained calm and welcomed him with his foot. Jiang Zonghuai commanded the three armies, breathing heavily as he entered Chen Bao's territory. Shen Meizhen drew his bow and nocked an arrow, but Hu Zongfan dived to save it.

▲ Qu Yue's Kick Decides the Game

Ma Zhishan worked hard, not only often pulling a rickshaw, but also being able to kick the ball out of bounds. After much commotion, the break arrived. After switching sides and fighting again, Old Ma came to the field, acting as an inspector, reducing the number of jokes. You came and I went, with opposing edges, without a victor. For nearly ten minutes, Chen Bao's front-line generals pressed extremely hard. Zhou Jicheng could not resist with two fists. Qu Yue spotted an opening, and with a kick, the ball flew like an arrow. Jiang Jianhou was caught off guard, and the score was opened. Although Xin Wen Bao worked hard to counterattack afterwards, time did not allow it. The game ended.

▲ Shen Bao and Current Affairs: One to One

The warm sun shone all over the baseball field. Three thousand faces with different emotions. A moment of laughter, a moment of noise. Mrs. Jiang Huaiqing frowned and said "It's slippery." It turned out that Huaiqing was in charge of goalkeeping, so it was really "slippery."

▲ Current Affairs' New Three Barefoot

Before there was Ma Hua's defender Yu Zhuohua repelling enemies barefoot, after there was Little Sister Mei Hong imitating, brave is brave, but still not as good as today's Current Affairs New Three Musketeers. Although the former was barefoot, they still had socks. Today's players are completely naked, without any pretense. Commander Jiang Xiangqing first revealed his nine-foot round skin, with momentum like a galloping horse. Xia Kaiming also rose to imitate. Li Zhuozhen learned from the threshold, taking consistent action with Old Jiang. Therefore, fans said, "It's like transplanting rice seedlings and like fishing," But they are still really playing soccer. Truly being barefoot takes a lot of advantage. The sole of the foot faces down, it is a special pair of shoes that ensures they won't fall. Therefore, Old Jiang runs particularly fast.

▲ Nie Shiqi Scores First

After a long time of close combat and hand-to-hand fighting, the two sides rebuilt their defenses. The Current Affairs new front line, under the command of Old Jiang, coordinated extremely well. Shen Bao's central defense had the general Xie Hong, who was good at using all eighteen weapons and was exceptionally brave. The third line of defense, Li Zunyong, blocked east and west, impenetrable. The ball lingered for a long time in the center line. Jiang Xiangqing dribbled south, breaking through three passes in a row, and at a suitable spot, passed the ball to Nie Shiqi, who advanced a few steps and shot powerfully into the goal. Shen Bao was defeated by 1 to 0 in the first half.

▲ Zhu Mingxin Returns the Favor

Shen Bao's center forward, Sun Daosheng, was a veteran on the field. How could he willingly be inferior and not think of resisting? In the second half, he encouraged the front-line generals to burn their boats and fight to the death. Xie Hong transported his wheels busily. The Current Affairs new defense roared like men and horses, shouting and killing. Jiang Xiangqing entertained his guests thoughtfully, either shaking hands with them or kicking them, without any mishaps for five minutes. But as the saying goes, "Things don't happen more than three times." Not long after Sun Daosheng raised the flag of righteousness, and ten thousand people followed his example. Lu Erqiang ferried the ball on his feet, and Zhu Mingxin found an opportunity to strike, hitting the key point. Although Current Affairs refused to compromise, the environment forced them to finally sign the agreement.

Heaven was not fair, raining for a day or two, turning the baseball field into a vast little sea. When the ball landed, the water splashed everywhere, like the January 28th bombs in Zhabei. You grabbed and I stole, and in the end, everyone measured the land. The snow-white pants changed color, and the soccer shoes were covered in mud, becoming one. We couldn't tell each other apart. With every step, mud followed the ball, splashing into the opponent's eyes, making it difficult to open them. Although it was not like drowned chickens, they turned into mud-plated Wuxi Afu. Inside the entire field, all twenty-two people became mud statues. Li Jun Zun was especially coated into a model, and when he got up, his face turned into a dragon and became a scholar of the Pavilion of Literature. Forty-four hands temporarily served as plasterers, slipping east and west, like ice skating on the North Sea.

Spring and Autumn

The Philosophy of Dice 206

— Zhan Lu

Dice are rumored to be the creation of Cao Zijian, who could compose poetry in seven steps. If this is true, dice are a product of the third century, roughly 1,700 years ago. Later, in the Tang Dynasty, manufacturing became more sophisticated, with bone carved into holes and painted with vermillion and ink. There were also clever designs with hidden patterns, such as embedding red beans into the holes, chosen for their bright and easily visible color. As Wen Tingyun's alluring poem goes: "In the exquisite dice are red beans set, does anyone know the longing in human bones?"

Based on the aforementioned history of dice, although it cannot be definitively determined that Cao Zijian invented dice, it can be asserted that it was a Chinese invention, not a Western one. However, there is still a question. I read Dai Hongci's "Travels in Nine Countries," where he visited the museum in Denmark and saw ancient artifacts dating back thousands of years. The most peculiar of these were stone dice, with dots representing the numbers one through six, arranged in the same manner as in China. Upon seeing this, Dai suspected that these were Chinese artifacts that had spread to this region. However, the museum director, Blinkenberg, vehemently denied this. If he vehemently denied it, then the invention of dice in China and the West was purely coincidental.

The numbers and arrangement of dice are quite consistent with philosophy, especially with Einstein's theory of relativity. The opposite of the greatest prosperity is the greatest decline; therefore, the opposite of six is one. Without reaching the peak of prosperity, the opposite will not be the depths of decline; therefore, the opposite of five is two. Being only slightly more prosperous, the opposite will also be only slightly more declined; therefore, the opposite of four is three.

The greedy gambler, after rolling the dice several times, wants the numbers to be even higher. Rolling a total of six is not enough; rolling a six and a five is not enough. He must roll a full six of everything. Alas! Reaching the peak is also reaching the depths of decline. Who knows, when it turns over, what the actual total number will be?

The Pawnbroker's Face 207

— Rong Yu

The poor, working-class friends often visit the pawnshop behind the poor man's door many times each month. And they all say in unison: "The pawnbroker's face is really hard to look at!" In fact, the pawnbroker is also a person with ears, eyes, mouth, and nose. They are by no means hideous and terrifying. But poor friends tell me: "Their faces are always iron-clad; their words are always decisive. Don't you think that's hard to look at? No shop, no business, ever has this kind of air. In business, they can be called a special zone."

Actually, the faces of Shanghai's pawnbrokers are still somewhat pleasing. Because on any road, there's a pawnshop every five steps, an appraisal every ten steps, the backdoor to convenience of the poor is full of openings. If you don't succeed with one owner, you can go to another, so pawnbrokers, for the sake of business, never make things too difficult for the poor. But it's not the same inland! Often, in a city or a town, there's only one or two. They've got you by the horns, where can you run to? So the pawnbroker's pretense is even easier to put on. They open at nine in the morning and close at four in the afternoon, just like a bank. Some inexperienced poor friends who try to pawn or redeem during their lunch break are in for bad luck. You're told to wait patiently, because they won't put down their rice bowls, and even if they're done eating, they'll wash their faces and smoke before starting to turn the pages. If a clueless friend were to rush them, they'd only get cursed at.

Thinking about it, some things aren't surprising. Whenever you seek something from someone, you must lower your head and humble yourself. Although a pawnshop isn't a charitable organization, it's still a creditor, and you always have to ask them for money. So, it's natural that they have a hard face to look at. In fact, there are many people in the world with faces like pawnbrokers! Friends in difficulty always say that they will share blessings and hardships. But when one of them prospers while the other still struggles, then the prospering friend will also put on a pawnbroker-like face. When you get a lover, gold and silver flow away like water, and of course you're exceptionally affectionate. But when the money runs out and you're left empty-handed, then the sweet face will also turn into a pawnbroker-like face. Besides, there are many things like this!

"Having to pass under their eaves, how can one not bow one's head?" Poor friends! Don't complain about the pawnbroker's hard face to look at, if you weren't poor, how would you ever see that awkward face?

A Grand Funeral 208

— Xu Xiaoting

When a person stretches out their legs and passes away, according to universal law, if the deceased made contributions to the world during their lifetime, we naturally mourn them or build some memorial to serve as an example for future generations. Otherwise, if the deceased was just an ordinary person, their death would be no different from the death of a cat or dog, unworthy of attention.

Those squatting on the boat of society, especially the rich merchants, big businessmen, officials, politicians, and misers, once they die, their descendants should, in theory, take out some of their wealth to do some public welfare for the society in order to leave a lasting memorial. However, the Chinese are extremely selfish. Society is society, and private affairs are private affairs. Public affairs are irrelevant to them!

Vanity shrouds the heads of all mankind. The so-called filial sons and virtuous grandchildren in our country are well aware that the wealth left by their ancestors was not used for society during their lifetime, and their descendants will certainly keep it for themselves to enjoy.

However, when their parents die, in order to praise the deceased's reputation and exaggerate their own filial piety, the most glorious and moving thing in their consciousness is a grand funeral. Among the decorations of the dead turning under the wheels of the city, a grand funeral is an extremely common, extremely ordinary, and extremely expensive thing.

Putting out rows of funerary objects, paper effigies, ceremonial attendants, and everything else stretching for several miles, spending thousands or even tens of thousands, the descendants are always happy and sincere, because this kind of approach can attract the attention of the crowd and the public's sight and sound. This kind of unconscious behavior, which the humans clinging to the Earth's crust engage in, only the Chinese are willing to do foolishly and stubbornly. A grand funeral is indeed a manifestation of a morbid mentality in Chinese society.

National Soul! 209

— Jie Lu

"What exactly is a human being? Please answer me!" This was what a solemn old pastor asked me. Originally, I was just a basic scholar who, due to my weak constitution and frequent illnesses, enjoyed perusing Buddhist and Taoist texts to study methods of nourishing my body. Later, through a friend's introduction, I came to know several Christians who fervently praised the gifts of their "Holy Spirit" and "God" to me. As I wanted to learn some Christian doctrines, I consulted that old pastor, but who knew that the old pastor would start by asking me this question.

I replied to the old pastor, "Taoism speaks of 'nature' and 'life'; nature is the spirit, and life is the physical body. Guiding and ingesting elixirs is to temper the physical body, while quiet sitting and breathing exercises are to cultivate the spirit. Therefore, a person is composed of these two things, 'nature' and 'life', and to increase longevity, one must focus on these two words. Buddhism says that a person is composed of the soul and the physical body, the physical body being a temporary combination of the four great elements: 'earth,' 'water,' 'wind,' and 'fire.' Therefore, all four elements are empty, and this stinking carcass will soon turn to nothing. Only the soul is immortal; the four births and six paths are clear evidence of the soul. I believe in both Buddhist and Taoist teachings. I think: a person's physical body is of course composed of carbon, iron, phosphorus, and organic compounds; the cells of our physical body are like millions of batteries; isn't the soul like an electron? A person is formed by combining various elements and electrons."

The old pastor smiled and said, "That is not so; a person is composed of three things: 'spirit,' 'soul,' and 'body.' God sculpted man from clay and breathed into him a soul, and the spirit is the last thing given. Only when this person turns to God, receives baptism, and vows to be a good person does God grant the 'spirit'!" After hearing the old pastor's words, I suddenly understood. Look at our fellow countrymen, in these days of "national peril," with the Northeast lost and the beacon fires of North China raging, yet the decadent atmosphere of the Southern Dynasties persists, with people indulging in sensual pleasures, their souls drifting away. They are reveling in lust and their souls are not attached to their bodies. Could this situation be the "national soul" of our Republic of China! Now, Tianjin and Beijing are in imminent danger, and North China is on the verge of collapse, which is to be expected. But must we wait for the desolate nights of autumn before the ghosts of the wronged and forsaken appear in our Jiangnan? God! Quickly grant the "spirit" to the Chinese people! Amen.

Long Novel

The Northeast Fourth Company Commander 210

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seven: Words Sever Affection, Doors Shut in Tearful Grief; Bearing Responsibility, Wine Shared in Discussion

Unexpectedly, Ji Zhi's whereabouts changed greatly, and he was not seen returning until five o'clock. The days were short in winter. By five o'clock, the sky was already pitch black. Even if the old maid had the determination to wait quietly, time would not permit it. So he returned despondently for two consecutive days. After ten days, he became somewhat impatient. When a maid from the Gan family came out to buy things, the two encountered each other, and he smiled: "Aunt Wang, you did a lot for me last year. I didn't even give you any money to spend during the New Year, I'm really sorry." As he spoke, he took out two small bills from his pocket and stuffed them into Aunt Wang's hand, smiling: "I don't have anything to give you, don't mind the small amount, take it and buy a packet of tea to drink." Aunt Wang unexpectedly received several bills from him and didn't know what he meant, but it's always a good thing when people give money, so she greeted Gui Zhi and thanked her repeatedly. Gui Zhi smiled: "You have so many people in your family, up and down, just you alone, it's really hard for you!" Aunt Wang said: "I'm used to it, it's nothing, I'm very comfortable." Gui Zhi said: "Is your master often at home?" Aunt Wang said: "The master is always away for most of the day." Gui Zhi pretended to be very natural, without any hesitation, and asked Aunt Wang: "What about your second master? Is he also away for most of the day?" When Aunt Wang heard him mention the second master, she looked at his face and smiled, the crow's feet under her eyes creasing into many layers. She smiled: "Miss, let me say a few words to you, but don't be angry." When Gui Zhi heard these words, her heart skipped a beat. However, his attitude remained very calm. He smiled: "Why would I be angry about your second master's affairs?" Aunt Wang, seeing that he didn't mind, told him in detail how the master came back and discussed with the madam, how the madam advised the master after the discussion, how the master told the madam to scare the second master, and how the second master admitted his mistake and wanted to break off contact with the old maid. Gui Zhi's face turned red and then pale when she heard these words, but she smiled: "It's your master and madam who are overthinking things. I'm just a young woman, why would I have any dealings with the masters?" This is just a one-time thing, don't tell anyone else about it in the future. (76)

Children's Paradise

Children's Toys 211

Gentlemen, today I have some very important words to say. These words come from famous child psychologists who have gained them through experiments in kindergartens. Therefore, parents must pay attention to the nature of their children and try to remedy any deficiencies in their home education. For example, with children's toys, we think of them as ordinary things, and we simply spend money to buy them for them to play with, regardless of whether they are good or bad, not knowing which kind of toy is suitable for which kind of child's nature. However, children in their early childhood, especially when their knowledge is gradually opening up, it is best to pay attention to their nature. If we understand their nature and slowly cultivate and influence them, then we can gradually reform their original bad qualities and remedy their shortcomings. Now, I will briefly explain what kind of toys should be given to children of different natures:

(1) For children who are nervous, they should be given gardening tools, sprinklers, wooden horses, balls, trumpets, drums, electric trains, and other toys.

(2) For children who are restless, they should be given picture albums, origami, paper cutting, string games, tangrams, and other toys.

(3) For children who lack independence, they should be given clay crafts, puzzle games, string games, and other toys.

(4) For children who lack patience, they should be given bean crafts, gardening tools, puzzle games, fishing gear, drawing templates, and other toys.

(5) For children who lack perseverance, they should be given sewing tools, kitchen tools, clay crafts, drawing templates, and other toys.

(6) For children who are timid, they should be given wooden horses, swings, stilts, bicycles, high jumps, long jumps, and other games.

(7) For children who are cruel, they should be given animal toys, insects, birds and beasts, fresh flowers, statues of gods and Buddhas, and other toys.

(8) For children who don't like to make friends, they should be given magic lanterns, spinning wheel games, Arhat idols, and other toys that involve groups.

(9) For children who are cunning and deceitful, they should be given toys of kind and compassionate idols of gods and Buddhas.

The Invention of the Telescope 212

Once upon a time, in a village in Italy, there was an eyeglass shop. The shop's apprentice often played with convex and concave lenses, and he found it very interesting. Sometimes he would hold a convex lens in each hand and look through them carefully, and he seemed to see things outside more closely than when he looked through just one lens. After the apprentice discovered this, he called the other apprentices in the shop to come and see. Sure enough, it was true. At this time, even the neighbors came to watch. A famous scholar named Galileo happened to be passing by when they were making a fuss. He didn't know why they were gathered together, snatching things to look at, so he also grabbed one to take a look and said, "What's so special about your convex lenses? Can I borrow them to take a look?" The apprentice, with a smug smile on his face, gave them to him. Sure enough, when he used both hands to move the convex lenses back and forth to look carefully, he could see things far away when the distance between the two lenses was far apart, and as he gradually moved them closer, he could see things closer. Therefore, after Galileo returned home, he focused on studying the principles behind it. As a result, he put the convex lens in a tube, made it telescopic, and invented the telescope.

Number Questions and Answers 213

— Chu

(Question) Wang Er is ten years old this year, and he wants his father to buy him a bicycle. His father said, "When my age is twice your age, I will definitely buy it for you." Now his father is forty years old, so when will Wang Er be able to buy the bicycle?

(Answer) When Wang Er is fifteen years old, his father will be forty-five years old, which is exactly three times Wang Er's age.

(Question) A merchant sold twenty jars of Shaoxing wine for eighty yuan. The next day, he bought them back for seventy yuan. On the third day, he sold these twenty jars of wine to others for ninety yuan. How much did this merchant earn, and how much did he earn per jar?

(Answer) He earned a total of twenty yuan, and he earned one yuan per jar.

(Question) Zhang Er looked at the clock at home and saw that it was eight o'clock when he went to the post office to deliver an urgent letter. When he arrived at the post office, he saw that the clock at the post office was eight fifteen. He immediately returned home by the same route. At this time, the clock at home was eight twenty. Is the clock at home fast or slow compared to the clock at the post office?

(Answer) He didn't delay at the post office and immediately returned by the same route, and he didn't run any faster or slower than when he went. It can be seen that the clock at home is five minutes fast.

Large Volume of US Cotton Traded 228

New York, May 19th telegram reports on the cotton market situation for the week: After German Chancellor Hitler's speech in Congress, raw cotton prices rose sharply, but soon there was a reaction trend, with reduced activity by buyers and gradually shrinking transaction volumes. Except for some areas in Texas and the northern and central cotton belt, the new cotton crop is progressing better this month, but it is still delayed by one to three weeks. There are continued reports of large-volume cotton transactions. It is reported that the cotton held by the Red Cross, except for approximately 170,000 bales stored in New York, has been dispersed. According to Washington news, the issue of how to receive the remaining old cotton that was previously stockpiled with government financial assistance is currently being discussed based on the installment sales terms of the rural relief plan. Regarding cotton field control under the rural relief plan, there is currently no concrete development, but Senator Smith, who initiated the installment sales plan, believes that this year's cotton season started late, so cotton fields can be reduced by five to six million acres.

Silk and Tea - The Weather Is Unfavorable and Silkworm Diseases Are Rampant

Jiangning 229

This year, farmers in various cities and villages have only raised about 50-60% of the silkworms compared to last year due to economic difficulties. However, the silkworm seeds were mostly improved varieties. In the Xiaodanyang area, some farmers, lacking the funds to purchase improved seeds, raised local varieties. The weather was initially very good, and with the assistance of instructors, the silkworms developed smoothly. The earliest local variety silkworms are now emerging, with some starting to spin cocoons. The improved variety silkworms are also in their fourth molt, eating vigorously. Unexpectedly, in recent days, there have been repeated thunderstorms, resulting in hot and humid conditions followed by sudden cold, causing climate imbalances and a sudden increase in humidity. The local variety silkworms, even with sufficient food, are delayed in emerging. The silkworms that have started spinning cocoons are breaking their silk due to the thunder. The vigorous foreign variety silkworms are also experiencing a sudden decrease in appetite, sluggish movement, and the development of hardened skin disease. There are reports of silkworms developing yellow excrement after eating leaves wet with rain, resulting in losses. As the silkworms are about to spin cocoons, this represents a failure at the final stage. The silkworm farmers are all crying out in despair. The instructors are currently trying to provide assistance by artificially adjusting the temperature and humidity and cleaning the silkworm rearing rooms and tools.

Hang County 230

In the Linping area, the early batch of local variety silkworms have suffered damage from the weather, with many remaining silkworms. Farmers are starting to raise improved varieties to compensate. The silkworms are eating vigorously, and the instructors are actively providing guidance. In addition, the weather is warm and favorable, and the development is very good. The early batch of local silkworms are in their major molt and eating vigorously, while the late batch of foreign variety silkworms are also in their third molt and eating sufficiently. However, in recent days, there have been consecutive thunderstorms, with hot and humid conditions followed by sudden cold, causing changes. The early silkworms of the local variety in the upper and lower four villages have developed black spots on their bodies (commonly known as maggot disease), as well as swollen bodies that rot and smell after death (commonly known as puffy disease). Even the foreign variety silkworms are eating less and developing white excrement. Some are experiencing yellow excrement after eating wet leaves and spitting out black liquid. The instructors are currently taking measures to remove diseased silkworms to prevent the spread of the disease, and are also adjusting the temperature and humidity in the silkworm rearing rooms in coordination with the silkworm farmers to provide careful rearing in the hope of making up for the losses.

Only local Zhuang needle tea and pearl tea items are in some demand from French traders. The trend of the tea market is quite pessimistic.

Wenzhou Merchants Arranging for the Loading of Foreign Rice 234

▲ 客秈運閩途沉六千包…閩辦暫停

Yesterday, Wenzhou merchants became active again, inquiring about foreign Ke Xian rice in the market. There was originally hope for an upward trend in the foreign Ke Xian rice market, but the Wenzhou merchants suddenly stopped buying. Recently, the Ke Xian rice market has been supported entirely by Fujian merchants. Once the Fujian merchants stop buying, the market immediately shrinks. The reason for the Fujian merchants' suspension yesterday was that 6,000 bags of Ke Xian rice that they had purchased the day before, loaded onto the He'an ship for transport to Fujian, sank after the ship was loaded and was turning to leave the dock, after being hit by a foreign merchant ship. All 6,000 bags of rice loaded were impossible to salvage. Some of the Fujian merchants had not purchased sufficient marine insurance, and were therefore seeking remedies. The merchants were unable to continue buying in the market yesterday, so the market was quiet. However, after this loss of 6,000 bags, the merchants will inevitably need to replenish their stock in the market in the coming days, so the trading outlook is optimistic. Yesterday, the Wenzhou merchants purchased 142 bags of Hunan coarse Qing rice for 6.65 yuan, and also purchased 1,000 bags of returned Xiaojiao rice from merchants for 7.60 to 7.58 yuan, an increase of 0.03 to 0.05 yuan compared to the previous market, due to the support of foreign merchants and optimistic sentiment. Mainland merchants also tried to purchase 200 bags of Hunan Pijing rice for 6.777 yuan. In addition, merchants from this street and Fujian merchants purchased 700 bags of Anhui Hunan Guanji rice for 6 yuan. Other transactions were not disclosed.

Marked Flour and Wheat Prices Plunge After Rising 235

After the flour market opened in the morning, prices for various months showed signs of rising, although the quoted price for foreign wheat was down by about 0.10 yuan. However, the market sentiment was influenced by the easing of tensions in Tianjin and the continuous torrential rains, which inevitably affected the prospects for new wheat. Therefore, after the opening prices, the market rose, with prices increasing by more than 0.01 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. Trading in various lots was also exceptionally brisk. It was reported that merchants from Yingkou were also buying, so the market was generally good. However, when the market opened in the afternoon, prices for various months plummeted again, due to rumors in the market that the situation in Tianjin had become chaotic, and the weather turning clear, which caused many speculators to sell off their holdings. In addition, large factories also began to sell, causing the market to decline further. Judging from the subsequent market conditions, if the situation in the north does change, the flour market will inevitably be difficult to recover. As a result, the current month's price fell by 0.0125 yuan compared to the previous day, the June price fell by 0.02 yuan, the July price fell by 0.015 yuan, the August price fell by 0.0025 yuan, the September price fell by 0.0005 yuan, and the October price fell by 0.01 yuan.

After the wheat market opened in the morning and afternoon, prices initially rose and then fell. In the morning, due to the continuous rain and cold weather, observers inside and outside the industry believed that the new wheat crop would be greatly discounted. In addition, the flour market was also doing well, and buying interest was strong. There were few sellers, and they were all raising prices. Therefore, prices for July, August, and September rose by 0.02, 0.03, and 0.04 yuan, respectively, compared to the previous day. However, in the afternoon, the market became quiet again. The weather had cleared, and the flour market had fallen back, causing opening prices to be unfavorable. Prices subsequently softened. As a result, the current month's price rose by 0.02 yuan, while the prices for August and September each fell by a small amount of 0.01 yuan. The remaining months did not open.

Free Talk

Escort 241

— Ying Pingdan

Whether it's socializing or writing articles, besides the host, there's always an "escort." Because with an escort, you feel lively and vivid; otherwise, it's lonely and you can't get up the interest.

"Those who have money contribute money; those who have strength contribute strength." On the surface, we see that contributing money is for saving the country, and contributing strength is also for saving the country. Looking at the current situation: contributing money and contributing strength are equally urgently needed, because the lack of equipment certainly requires money. At the same time, a weak military force, especially, requires strength. In fact, this view still hasn't grasped the deep meaning of the article writer. If you understand it, you'll surely know: "Those who have money contribute money" is the host; "Those who have strength contribute strength" is the guest. Because needing money is the main point of the article, while needing strength is just written casually, not the main meaning of the text.

Although I dare not boast of "understanding books in between," I can dare to admit that "understanding the heart is not far away." Because reading similar articles is not new to me. For example, the previous "Saving the country by storing money," "Saving the country by redeeming roads," "Saving the country by ××," etc., all used this same writing style.

If someone says I'm arbitrary, or laughs at my paranoia, then I can frankly say: Regarding "those who have money," isn't there a very meticulous opening of a "contributing money" path for them—saving the country through aviation? But what about the "strength" aspect? Aren't those "powerful" people who really want to "contribute strength" still clenching their fists and waiting with a belly full of anger?

Under the Stove 242

— Mou Zhui

— Rural Life Sketch

The spatula keeps shoveling, with a "chachacha" sound, mixed with the "lili lala" sounds of mustard greens in the pot.

Aunt Shen, with her hair disheveled, strands of hair sticking to her oily forehead.

"What's wrong? Burn it hotter!" She put down the spatula and shouted towards the stove door, wiping the sweat on her forehead with her sleeve.

There was no answer. The fire starter, Lai Tou Agou, was curled up at the stove door, looking like a tailor, lying there blowing on the fire. But hard beans couldn't be lit for a while. Agou hurriedly tried to find matches, but unexpectedly a puff of white smoke came out of the stove, shining brightly, the bean shells burst, the fire liver was on fire; the fire tongue rolled out of the stove door, wrapping and wrapping, Lai Tou Agou's newly shaved shiny head and a black face, were illuminated by the fire tongue, and glowing brightly.

The pot screamed again, lili lala.

Chachacha! The spatula kept shoveling. Aunt Shen, her head and face immersed in the green steam, pouting her little lips, her eyes wrinkled, and completely covered with tears.

"Little devil!" She couldn't help stamping her feet and screaming: "When it's not hot, it's not hot, but when it's hot, it's all at once!"

Agou still didn't make a sound, holding a large piece of cold ash and pressing it on the raging fire.

Aunt Shen skillfully added sugar, soy sauce, and wine, and put on the pot lid.

But another pot lid was opened. White steam was flying, flying, and the fragrance of meat spread throughout the kitchen. Looking at the pieces of meat in the pot, she, Aunt Shen, remembered her mother-in-law's instructions:

"You can't cook too much meat, or there won't be any big pieces left. These servants, they all drag the big pieces into their bowls, they're not people who appreciate good food... Meat prices are so expensive, and they add water... We can't cut the pieces too big anymore. It's too hard to farm now!..."

But today's meat pieces are overcooked. "Agou, little devil, it's my bad luck to have this little devil cooking!" She complained in her heart.

"One, two, three, four: one, two, three, ... four pieces per person, thirty-two pieces in a bowl,...

Aunt Shen counted in her heart, filling three large bowls with meat pieces.

The pot lid of the mustard greens was opened again. Scooping up some vegetable soup, she brought it to her lips, blew on it, took a sip, pursed her lips, and wrinkled her brow:

"Too bland."

Muttering, she grabbed a handful of salt and threw it into the pot. On the stove surface, copper spoons, spatulas, oil bottles, dishcloths, vegetable bowls... were placed haphazardly.

"Salty vegetable soup, bean sprouts, mustard greens, meat, all four are here!" She glared at the vegetable bowls on the stove: "Agou, little devil!" She shouted sharply, "Are you comfortable sitting there? Hurry up and get the wine, and take the vegetable bowls out. The field workers are coming back to eat."

Aunt Shen hurriedly cleared a space on the stove surface, picked up a rice basket and put it down, removed the lid of the rice pot, and then took a spatula from the knife rack, mixing the white rice and wheat bran into the basket. Her face, steamed in the hot air of the rice, finally showed a smile:

"Okay, just waiting for the field workers to come back to eat."

She breathed a sigh of relief.

In the Wheat Field 243

— Zhou Guangxi

It was that time again when the wheat ears grew to half a person's height. Little Gouzi didn't even graze the cow. He stood on the edge of the wheat field, staring blankly at the setting sun.

He knew that Xiao Qiao'er would pass by his field at this time every day, because it should be the time for Xiao Qiao'er to go back from the fields. He thought that he wouldn't let this little girl run away this time. Every time she stirred up his anger, she would slip away, laughing at him from afar.

Xiao Qiao'er really came, stepping on her own long shadow. She greeted Little Gouzi with a smile. Little Gouzi followed her from the edge of the wheat field, and Little Gouzi started singing.

Clever girl's head is like a foreign building,

Clever girl's feet are like cow horns,

Clever girl's hands are like steamed buns,

Clever girl's waist is like a rush bag,…

Xiao Qiao'er scolded him: "You wag your tongue, you scold your auntie..." Little Gouzi laughed, but he didn't answer. He kept singing.

Clever girl's back is like bean curd sheets,

Clever girl's shoulders are like soap pods,

Clever girl's eyes are like morning stars,

Clever girl's breasts are like…

Xiao Qiao'er said, "I'll hit you, tear your mouth," and she turned around to grab his little braid. He reached out and touched her chest, and his hand slipped further down. Xiao Qiao'er got anxious and grabbed his braid to fight with him. He hugged her waist, and the two of them rolled from the edge of the wheat field into the wheat patch.

The sun had already set, and a vast twilight covered the earth. As the evening breeze passed, the wheat ears rippled like water waves. A few clusters of wheat ears, trembling urgently, were also slowly hidden by the darkness.

× × × × ×

The next morning, the dew was not yet dry, and Little Gouzi followed his father past this wheat field. His father discovered a pile of wheat that had been trampled down in the wheat field. "Damn it," he cursed, "Another little bastard, without a mother or father, has nowhere to have fun, and comes to have fun in my wheat field. Gouzi, go and pick it up."

Little Gouzi blushed and silently went to fix the broken wheat roots. He thought of Xiao Qiao'er, and everything that happened in this place yesterday evening, and he became confused again.

"What are you spacing out about? Hurry up and leave!" His father roared at Little Gouzi. How could an old man understand a young man's thoughts?

Qu Lu Ramblings 244

— Zi Zhan

(31) Fart Literature

Japanese person Fukutomi Oribe wrote the book "Fart," which compiles all the literature about farts, up to 200,000 words. Among them, the most important are the science of farts, famous fart people throughout history, Hiraga Gennai's masterpiece ("Theory on Farting, Examination of Bent Farts"), the comedies and tragedies of farts, as well as legends, fairy tales, jokes, and crazy songs related to farts. It can be said to be the culmination of fart literature, and it is indeed unique throughout history. Domestic scholars have translated many Japanese books, but this book is missing, which is a pity. However, perhaps Mr. Wu Zhihui's article can replace it, so that there is no regret? In the article "What We Petition to Mr. Zhang Shizhao," Mr. Wu recounted that when he was 31 years old, he returned home from Beijing, and found a book called "How Can This Be Reasonable" on a small book stall. As soon as he opened it, he said, "Fart, fart, it's really unreasonable." Suddenly, he realized that he should despise the literati and not become one. Even if he was involved in writing, he would do it with the spirit of "fart, fart, it's really unreasonable." ...But there was a dull clerk in a small shop, working as a proofreader at the Shanghai Medical Bookstore, who borrowed 700 yuan and searched for the dog farts that I had scattered in newspapers and magazines, and even found the school essays from thirty years ago and engraved a collection of essays. That's really terrible..." It can be seen that Mr. Wu's writing, he claimed to be "farting," and it was "dog farts" rather than human farts. He had the cleverness of self-awareness, which was a great exaggeration for writers. It is precisely this old man's inability to achieve this. Unfortunately, the Chinese people do not understand humor. Doctors and scholars regard Mr. Wu as one of the greatest thinkers of China in the past three hundred years, revolutionary comrades regard Mr. Wu as a theorist in the party, and newspaper reporters even strongly invite Mr. Wu to talk and write articles. This is exactly what Mr. Wu called "really terrible." Dr. Liu Fu once punctuated and published the book "How Can This Be Reasonable" (i.e., He Dian), recommending it as Mr. Wu's teacher in writing. Although he has a way to make money, he is also unreasonable in farting. Yuan Jiang Zhengzi's Mountain House Random Notes records that Lin Guanguo of Sanshan, at the age of seven, roamed the city and claimed to sell plans. Someone jokingly asked him to chant about turning arrow qi, and he wrote the poem:

Look at it and you can't see it, named Xi,

Listen to it and you can't hear it, named Yi.

It's as if it came from its mouth,

Everyone covers their noses and passes by.

The so-called turning arrow qi, other books may write it as turning loss of qi, which is wrong. Arrow in the Book of Han is written as shit, and ancient shit and arrow are interchangeable. Arrow qi is a fart, it is the qi of the arrow. Turning is a verb, the same nature as letting go. The medical book says that the lower jiao spills qi, which belongs to this qi. In a slightly more scientific way, it can be said that it is the stinky gas discharged from the intestines and stomach. If you say it is a fart, the language is not elegant, and Western-dressed gentlemen and high-class Chinese people seem to find it difficult to say. Lin Guanguo's poem on turning arrow qi has a title that seems turbid, but the words are elegant. This is the best of fart articles. Lin Guanguo was a child prodigy, while Mr. Wu Zhihui can be called a holy old man, and Mr. Liu Fu is a dignified doctor. I am discussing farting, and I am honored to be able to look up to them and have something to do with them.

After writing this article, I remembered that when I was at "Dongda," I once listened to Mr. Gu Shi's lecture on philology. He wrote a pictographic dog character on the blackboard, and then wrote the four characters "Hu Shi's Literary Collection" in large letters at the root of the dog's tail. Those who saw it laughed in the hall.

Carrot Top's Whiskers 245

— Jules Renard, translated by Lin Quzuo

Back and Forth (Continued)

Afterward, she kissed him on the forehead, lest he be jealous.

The arrival of the holidays made Carrot Top so happy that he actually burst into tears. He was often like that; he often expressed his emotions incorrectly.

On the day school started (the date was Monday morning, October 2nd; starting with the Mass of the Holy Spirit), Mrs. Lepic, listening from afar to the bells of the public carriage, bent down and hugged her children tightly. Carrot Top was not included in this embrace. He earnestly hoped that it would be his turn, his hand already reaching for the strap above the carriage, the farewell words already prepared, he was so mournful that even his voice changed.

"Goodbye, my mother," he said, feigning a solemn expression.

"Hey, what do you take me for, you clown?" Mrs. Lepic said. "Would you lose money by calling me 'Mama' like everyone else? Who has ever seen such a thing? A child who still smells of milk trying to act grown-up is truly strange!"

But she still kissed him on the forehead, lest he be jealous.

Pen

The Saint Marc school, where Mr. Lepic sent his eldest son, Felix, and Carrot Top to board, had students who attended public middle school. They took the same walk four times a day. On beautiful spring and autumn days, this walk was very pleasant; even on rainy days, because the distance was very short, the young men would only feel cool and would not get soaked. So, this kind of walk was very beneficial to the body year-round.

This morning, they were returning from middle school again, walking slowly like sheep. Carrot Top, who was looking down and moving forward, suddenly heard someone say:

"Carrot Top, look, your father is over there!"

Mr. Lepic liked to surprise his children like this. He didn't write to inform them before he came. He let them suddenly see him, standing on the sidewalk across the street, his hands behind his back, a cigarette in his mouth.

Carrot Top and his older brother Felix jumped out of the line and ran to their father.

"Really!" Carrot Top said, "Even though I was thinking about someone, it wasn't about you."

"You only think about me when you see me," Mr. Lepic said.

Carrot Top wanted to say a few affectionate words, but he was so flustered that he couldn't think of anything. He stood on his tiptoes, wanting to hug and kiss his father. The first time, his lips touched his mustache. But Mr. Lepic seemed to deliberately avoid him, mechanically raising his head. Then he bent down again and leaned back, wanting to kiss Carrot Top on the cheek, but he didn't reach it. He only touched his nose. His kiss missed. He didn't push further, but he felt strange in his heart, wondering why his father would treat him like this.

"Does Dad not like me?" he thought. "I saw him hug and kiss my older brother Felix. He let him hug and kiss him, he didn't avoid him. Why is he dodging me? Does he want to make me jealous? I always feel like I miss my parents very much if I don't see them for three months. I was ready to jump on their necks like a puppy. We mutually enjoy each other's caresses as much as possible. But as soon as I see them, it makes me feel half cold."

Because he only wanted to think about these things sadly, Carrot Top didn't answer Mr. Lepic's questions properly. At this time, Mr. Lepic asked him if he had made any progress in Greek.

Carrot Top: It depends on which aspect. It's easier to translate Greek into French than to translate French into Greek. Because when translating Greek into French, we can guess some of the meaning. (To be continued)

Amateur Musings

The Struggle After Losing a Country is Very Difficult! 246

— Pu

Recently, someone said: "The majority of Chinese people have a very small concept of the nation, and in recent years, the general trend has been to blindly admire the sights, sounds, and goods of foreigners. Apart from the antiques of Peking, the Chinese people do not cherish or protect anything that is originally Chinese. Under this mentality, the Chinese nation must experience the pain of losing its country once, otherwise, it will probably not be easy to rise 'in time.'" This argument is undoubtedly a painful and heartbreaking criticism, but what we must pay attention to is whether it is easy to "rise" after experiencing the pain of losing a country?

According to recent reports in Japanese newspapers about the Korean independence movement: about 30 officials and police officers from the Osaka Port Police Station recently searched the home of Korean Zhang Shiyuan, who runs a maritime transport business in the port area, and arrested 40 people, including Hyun Gil-young, the head of the East Asia Navigation Cooperative, Kim In-dong, the clerk of the Jeju Island route Fubuki Maru, and Shen Won-sik, the cargo manager, as well as two young girls. They were interrogated by the Osaka Prefecture Special Criminal Higher Section and determined that Hyun Gil-young and others had an organization for the independence movement, and the East Asia Navigation Cooperative was its organizational body. The East Asia Navigation Cooperative was established 13 years ago with funds raised by Korean expatriates, calling on people from their hometown to travel on hometown ships. They purchased the Fubuki Maru and organized a shipping company. Currently, it has more than 500 members. Recently, they took advantage of the crowded Osaka pier on the 1st and 16th of each month to distribute various radical leaflets promoting the restoration of Korea, which attracted the attention of the police, who were on high alert and recently made arrests.

In recent years, we have often heard news of the Japanese breaking up Korean independence movement organizations. Each time there is a crackdown, there is always bloodshed and sacrifice by some Korean patriots. This relentless independence movement really fills us with infinite emotion and shame. Thinking about how easy it was for the Japanese to destroy Korea back then, and how difficult it is for Koreans to try to restore their country today, this is indeed a fact that those who are complacent and have not yet become slaves of a lost country should deeply reflect on.

Amateur Restaurant Police Life Small Special Issue (Part 1) The police are hosting guests at this restaurant today

Substitute 247

— Lin Jieyu

Candidate Police Officer

Life is moving forward with difficulty, and fate is playing with me. I have drifted to the land of × like floating clouds and flowing water. With the active efforts of my loyal friend Lao Wu, I am preparing to be introduced to a small city nearby to serve as a police officer. But Lao Wu didn't have time to go, so he asked Mrs. Wu to take me, because Mrs. Wu also had some connections with the head of the public security bureau. Mrs. Wu reluctantly agreed, and I immediately acted like a sensible servant, respectfully serving her on her journey.

When we arrived there, the bureau chief was not at home, and the bureau chief's wife was not there either, but the bureau chief's daughter was at home, a sallow-faced, low-browed, lifeless young lady who greeted us woodenly. After waiting for a long time, the bureau chief returned. He asked about my experience, frowned, and said a lot of "there's no way." Finally, after countless headshakes and regrets, he said with a sigh: I hereby appoint so-and-so as a probationary policeman at the × police station, and you must comply and report for duty immediately.

A probationary policeman, he has to eat on his own, sitting here

Page 20

waiting for a vacancy to become a formal policeman. If other policemen have illnesses or weddings and funerals, he can substitute, earning 24 copper coins per shift.

I actually lived like this for two months, which is also a very memorable thing in my short life!

Yin-Yang Blessed Land 248

— Yan Meizhuang

Police Officer

I am a young man who has received secondary education, an intellectual who is weak and unable to truss a chicken, but now I have actually run to the land of × to become a policeman, replacing the pen with a gun.

Our police station is located in a temple. When I was first led to this place, the goddess with three eyes greeted me with a humble smile. The name of the temple cannot be found. I only saw a signboard above it, arrogantly writing the four characters "Yin-Yang Blessed Land," which made me shudder and think of this as the edge of life and death. The temple is full of goddesses and little ghosts, and the air is filled with an incongruous atmosphere of tenderness and barbarity. The walls are covered with enigmatic paintings: a tiger with a big tail, a pointed mouth, small eyes, and covered in fur; a monk with a dog crawling on his head; a person with a head growing out of their navel; a dazed-looking man wearing broken shoes, with a sparrow flying out of his mouth: everything makes one feel the mystery and melancholy of life.

There are seven people in the station: a patrol leader, a cook, two gate guards, and three street guards. The patrol leader, the cook, and another brother are all locals; the rest: one from Guangxi, two from Zhili, and one from Hubei. The patrol leader is a big guy with thick eyebrows and large eyes, looking like a battle-ax made of meat; but the sound of his voice is like a broken gong that cannot be struck. The cook is the exact opposite, as thin as a reed, clenching his teeth all day long and not opening his mouth, as if he had sworn an oath never to speak. The other one is a drunkard who indulges in distiller's grains, with a bald head and a red face that constantly emits steam, muttering indistinctly, one can tell at a glance that he is soaked in liquor. The four outsiders are all tall and gaunt. They are all farmers who enjoy guarding their fields and being self-sufficient. The storms of history swept them away from their hometowns, and finally, they settled in this desolate corner. Life passes silently, and they twist and turn on the edge of hunger and death in silence. Usually, they seem to be nonchalant: laughing loudly, spitting everywhere, excitedly talking about someone else's "wife" and her affair with a monk. But when someone inadvertently mentions words like "hometown," "parents," "family," they immediately become quiet; and become old, weak: their heads droop, their hands hugging their knees, their chins resting on them, silently staring at the ground, sadness suffocating them!

At night, because there was no room for the other brothers to sleep, I slept in the main hall, finding two high and low tables to replace the bed. The fat patrol leader kindly found me a broken mattress. The blue-black cloth surface was covered with dust and grease, and the dark holes exuded a stuffy stench, and it seemed as if countless caterpillars were wriggling inside. The main hall was empty and vast, piled with lime and broken tiles, and filled with the breath of dampness, soil, and decaying wood, suggesting decay and disease. In front of the statue, incense ash and candle tears lingered, like a helpless old woman, sadly shedding her endless tears.

Darkness crept in through the holes in the window lattices, filling the main hall, and the eternal light slowly emitted a dim flame 丨丨 it is always silent during the day. The streamers in front of the statue 丨 congealed by cobwebs and dust 丨 issued a faint sigh in the air, resenting its eternal idleness and loneliness.

There are two goddesses, two deities, and eight little ghosts in front of my bed. The goddesses always have gentle smiles; the deities are full of petty bourgeois sentiments, sadly lamenting the decline of their majesty. As for those little ghosts, they are all the same, holding bamboo sticks in their hands, feathers of pheasants on their heads, full of fierce faces and rogue air; looking at the short railing in front of them that hinders their actions with an evil gaze, expressing their infinite anger.

The cold wind blew in from the holes in the window lattices, and the flame of the eternal light became drowsy. Old mice and small mice ran around in groups, calling and sniffing everywhere. In the air, coldness, like an invisible ghost, crept into the broken quilt to attack my body, and my body temperature was quickly sucked away by it.

The light in the main hall was as thin as hell, the spirits of darkness crawled everywhere, the murals floated like ghosts, and the turbidity of the air suffocated people. I was thrown into this "blessed land" to enjoy myself by what strange fate, I couldn't help but laugh loudly as I slept on the uneven bed.

Small Monograph

Talking About Scientific Management 249

— Hengyuan

Under the extreme panic of capitalist economy, in order to save the economic crisis and recession, there must be new and higher technologies and plans to understand and apply to increase economic efficiency, so as to eliminate the various wastes in the past economy and return it to a state of recovery. Therefore, scientific management has become an inevitable product, first advocated by American iron factory technician Taylor, and later studied by many politicians, industrialists, and bankers, it gradually became popular and put into practice. It was then successively adopted by countries such as England and Germany, and became a temporary savior in the economic world of the entire capitalist world. Since scientific management has become an important factor in the entire capitalist economy, the importance of its significance can be imagined. According to general statements, scientific management is a technique and plan application that promotes economic improvement. Its purpose is to improve the quality of goods, increase the quantity of goods, reduce the cost and price of goods, and enrich the welfare of the national economy, so it is an economic, progressive, and functional thing.

In capitalist countries, generally speaking, the first problem of scientific management is the concentration of capital, which is also called the union movement. The method of union is divided into vertical and horizontal types. Vertical union is the union of organizations related to production methods, linking from the acquisition of raw materials to the manufacture of goods into a system. Horizontal union is the union of organizations with the same production nature, that is, all production institutions in the same industry are united to reduce consumption and waste, increase production efficiency, and seek a large amount of profit. Its second problem is the standardization of production methods. The first step is to handle it in a company, the second step is to handle special industries in a region by New Dica, the third step is to handle it nationwide, regardless of the nature of the industry, by Contern, and the fourth step is to jointly establish an international standards association internationally. The purpose is to (1) obtain the greatest labor efficiency with the least effort, (2) reduce various different styles of goods as the basis (styles are different but there is no obvious benefit), study manufacturing methods, (3) eliminate the consumption of raw materials and power, (4) simplify the distribution of goods, (5) eliminate unnecessary transportation, excessive financial burdens, and useless intermediaries. According to this, (1) in the social aspect, the standard of living can be improved, and stability can be increased, (2) in the consumption aspect, prices can be reduced, and goods can be more in line with needs, (3) in the producer aspect, production can be fairly distributed and its benefits can be obtained, so that it can be coordinated and parallel with centralized capital.

However, judging from the international economic situation in recent years, the result of scientific management in capitalism has not resolved the crisis of capitalism. According to Varga's research, at least the international economic competition has not been reduced by international scientific management, and due to the fall in the price index, the profits of capital are still unsuccessful, and it is necessary to reduce wages and lay off workers domestically, so that the real wages of workers are falling day by day, and the number of unemployed people is increasing day by day. On the other hand, it also increases workers' diseases and disasters, and inevitably leads to a general shortening of workers' lives and a reduction in the period of labor capacity. Therefore, the lives of most workers are declining day by day, which reduces the purchasing power of the majority and makes the sales channels in the domestic market more difficult, forming a phenomenon of overproduction. Moreover, after capital is concentrated, taking advantage of domestic and foreign monopolies, even when production costs are obviously reduced, prices are not reduced, but prices are maintained at the same level, thereby increasing its profits. The so-called scientific management movement is really full of deep contradictions.

However, the modern form of scientific management is by no means accidental. It is the logical development of all capitalist production tendencies, and it is the clearest form of phenomenon. Needless to say, it is the final manifestation of capitalist development, a characteristic of the period of capitalist decline and disintegration.

In short, scientific management itself is still a kind of societal philosophy, principles, and appropriate basic technology, and its value is not harmed by the opposite results brought about by the application of capitalism. Once the right to industrial management is transferred from capitalists to all workers, it will undoubtedly exert its maximum efficiency and seek the happiness of all mankind.

Academic Arts and Literature

Mud Doll 250

— Li Peilin

This day, when we were having lunch, the side dishes had not yet been brought out. I first occupied the head of the table and hummed "Si Lang Visits His Mother". My younger sister sat at my left, pouting her lips, holding chopsticks in her mouth, and rattling her teeth. She was angry with me because I refused to let her play with the mud doll that I had made by hand in school. But after a while, we made up because our mother was late in coming out of the kitchen. My younger sister and I competed to see who could make the spoon louder with chopsticks, to see who was more skilled, until our mother brought out the dishes.

As we were eating, my cousin rushed in from outside. I understood his intention, but before he could say it, I still hoped that the words he said would not be guessed by me, but he finally said to my mother the words that I didn't want him to say:

"The money shop that I recommended to my cousin will welcome the God of Wealth the day after tomorrow. My cousin must go in tomorrow. That money shop is a Yuan-numbered shop with 50,000 capital. Six tables of food are served for each meal!"

He seemed to use all his strength to say these two sentences. Then, he said: "With such a large scope, there must be several tea boys. My cousin may not have to pour the spittoon when he goes in."

"So, I don't have to go to school this afternoon?" I dropped my chopsticks and stared at my mother.

"My cousin could have stopped going to school a long time ago," my cousin said. "This way, tomorrow morning at 8:30, I will definitely accompany my cousin to the shop. You must prepare the bedding and luggage in advance. Also, don't forget to buy a pair of incense and candles, which are to be used to worship the teacher. My cousin's teacher is the deputy manager of that money shop."

My cousin sat for a while and left. The room was quiet with only the three of us left, all silent. I had no heart to eat the remaining half bowl of rice. My younger sister, although she didn't understand, also looked very gloomy, but after a while, she said:

"Brother, you are going to be an apprentice tomorrow, so you don't need that mud doll anymore. Can you give it to me?"

I nodded. My mother remained silent, only looking at me carefully from head to toe with moist tears. A kind of indescribable sad emotion pressed on my heart 丨 I, who has always had a strong personality, couldn't help but fall into my mother's arms and cry.

"Good child," my mother stroked my hair and said; "Don't be like this, you are grown up, you should act like an adult, why do you cry when you hear that you are going to be an apprentice? Didn't my cousin say just now? That money shop is very big, you won't suffer when you go in. Child, three years is very fast, when you have learned the business, Mom will be waiting here for you to earn ingots back."

I raised my head and looked at my mother's face. She put on an unnatural smile, stroked my face with her fingers, and said:

"A fifteen-year-old still wants to hide in Mom's arms and act up, aren't you ashamed?"

But her eyes were filled with more tears than mine. I swallowed a mouthful of saliva, my heart was sore, and tears flowed like a waterfall. I remember very clearly that since my father died, I had never cried so sadly. But if my father had not died at that time, how could I have been forced to be someone else's apprentice, and how could I have had this painful cry today? Writing this, my father's gentle face could not help but appear before my eyes again.

Dinner passed hastily under the shroud of such a tragic atmosphere. I really wanted to eat a little more because this was my last dinner at home, but I finally ate one bowl less than usual.
