International Broadcasting Radio Station

The Current Situation of Soviet Working Women 253

— Speaker Fan Xin

Shop assistants, apprentices, workers, and all other readers of this publication! Today, I have the opportunity to talk to you about the general living conditions of Soviet working women. I am truly honored!

Soviet working women are completely equal to men in all aspects.

The October Revolution liberated Soviet women from the shackles of managing household affairs and taking care of children, and they all went to factories or rural areas to work like men.

In factories, the work performance of working women often exceeds that of men. They adopted socialist competitions and commando teams to increase the rate of production and improve labor methods. They often put forward various practical and specific opinions to contribute to the factory committee.

Liberated working women initially only hoped to overcome illiteracy. However, after being able to read and write, they had even greater desires. They needed to acquire political knowledge, technical knowledge, cultural knowledge, etc., because they knew that they were the builders of a new life and a new world, the builders of a socialist society. After work, they mostly went to clubs for entertainment and sports, or to libraries or schools to study.

Page 21

. They didn't want to waste a minute. Naturally, they also had to fall in love. However, they had principled regulations regarding love, which was based on not hindering work or study. If anyone spent too much effort on love, they would be criticized by the public.

No country in the world has laws that can protect working women like the Soviet Union, especially the protection of motherhood. Working women have a total of four months of recuperation before and after childbirth, during which time their wages are still paid. After this period, when they return to work in the factory, night work, excessive work, or relatively heavy work are all prohibited for her until after a considerable period. The necessities for infants are provided by the state within nine months of birth. When working women with children go to work in factories, they can put their children in nurseries, which are established by the state or the factory where she works. There, knowledgeable teachers and experienced nannies will take care of the children so that mothers can work with peace of mind.

In short, the Soviet government has used nurseries, kindergartens, children's homes, public canteens, public laundries, and various cooperatives to liberate them from the daily life constraints of being a "virtuous wife and good mother."

The wages of Soviet working women are determined based on their level of skill. The Soviet Union provides workers with all kinds of conveniences, such as rent, food, and other necessities. Workers can obtain them at a lower price than non-workers. Moreover, every working woman has at least two weeks of vacation each year, with wages still paid. Therefore, even if the wages of Soviet working women may not be as high as those of working women in the golden United States, in essence, due to the above reasons, they exceed what is obtained by oppressed and exploited working women in various capitalist countries. Moreover, by the end of the second five-year plan, the standard of living will be increased by two or three times.

Special Self-Employment Introduction

The Qualification Problem of a Poor Kid 254

— Ms. Shen Airong

I am a junior high school graduate. In the autumn of 1931, I was admitted to the kindergarten normal school attached to Jinan University. Unfortunately, the Shanghai War broke out, and Zhenru became a war zone. The kindergarten normal school, which had only been established for a few months, died prematurely, and I also lost my education. It has been a year and a half since then.

A few days ago, I got a very good news from a friend that students from the previous kindergarten normal school can be inserted into senior high school normal school, but they need to pay fees according to the general courses. This is such gratifying news! However, where does a member of the proletariat like me get this huge sum of money (the hostel fees and tuition fees for the previous kindergarten normal school were waived, only the meal expenses were not waived)? Although the amount is only sixty or seventy yuan, it is nothing to the rich merchants who spend thousands of dollars on smiles, and the wealthy officials who are wrapped in hundreds of thousands, but in the eyes of us poor people, it is a very large amount. Should I borrow from friends? I have never borrowed half a penny from anyone in my life, and I am really ashamed to open my mouth. Moreover, whether they believe you or not is still a question. And the relatives all say: What books are such big girls reading? It is more proper to learn some female handicrafts at home and marry early. Should I not read? Such a good opportunity, missing it is really too regrettable, because Jinan University is national, and those with scores above 75 points can be completely free, which is indeed good news for a poor kid like me. Moreover, I have had enough of the suffering of being trapped by qualifications. People without a high school diploma have to run into snags everywhere. In the past year, I don't know how much anger I have suffered for the sake of employment. No, this is the karma of a poor kid, who told you to ask for help from others? Without any brothers-in-law, younger uncles, or old uncles serving in the agency, you won't have a share in this vase-like, aristocratic position. Should I be a primary school teacher? But without registering, no matter how rich your knowledge is, you will always not be able to eat this bowl of noble leftovers. Should I be a clerk? I can't find the door. Should I be a lawyer? I don't have the aura of some legal scholars. Should I be a female worker? It is related to the face of the family. Should I be a dancer? That is not a proper female profession at all. As for the recruitment advertisements in the newspapers, I have also applied, but the letters are like the Yellow Crane never returning, and the response is like the ocean sinking, nothing more than promoting two-cent stamps for the post office. This is all because I suffer from not having qualifications, so I must become self-reliant only after graduating from high school. But I am just a poor kid, unable to do what I want, and therefore I am anxious, depressed, and disappointed. There are still three months before the start of the semester. I want to find a job, no matter how big or small, high or low, in these three months. If I can accumulate a sum of thirty to fifty yuan from this, it seems that it will be of no small help to the tuition fees for the second half of the year. Please forward the reply through this publication.

Little People's Parliament

How Should Workers Maintain Their Lives When Yarn Factories Reduce Working Hours? 255

— Discussant and Parliamentarian Yi Ping

China's pitifully immature national industry is always in a position of utter defeat. Recently, due to the dumping of foreign goods and overproduction, it has deeply felt that it has reached the end of its rope and cannot maintain its business. It has no choice but to implement a two-day reduction in working hours per week in order to save itself. At the same time, Japanese-owned companies in the country, also due to the result of China and India boycotting Japanese goods, have overproduction and have begun to implement reductions in working hours. After this news spread, it aroused the attention of many people in society. It can be seen that the seriousness of this issue is no less than that of all other issues.

The result of reducing working hours will undoubtedly have a great impact on the workers. In fact, although "three shifts are reduced per week, each worker actually only reduces one shift, and only four or five shifts per month, each shift's wages are 60 cents, which is only worth more than two yuan," in the world's lowest-wage country, the standard of living is exactly the opposite, becoming higher day by day. The result of workers selling their blood and sweat every month is that they are generally on the verge of starvation for the lowest life. This sum of more than two yuan is tantamount to depriving the workers of one-half or even the entire portion of their monthly wages to make up for the losses of the capitalists. Moreover, the lives of Chinese people are mostly built on the foundation of extended families. Behind every worker is the burden of an extended family. The unemployment of one worker will immediately affect the livelihood of the entire family. If most of the workers become unemployed as a result, what kind of phenomenon will occur in society? That is really unimaginable.

Recently, due to the destruction of the countryside, the decline in people's purchasing power, and the seizure of the virgin land in the Northeast, the original market for national goods will inevitably shrink, so there is also a so-called phenomenon of overproduction. However, according to the actual situation, it is exactly the opposite. According to last year's survey, the total number of spindles in the country was only 4,516,898, while Chinese-owned companies only had 2,589,040, accounting for about 57.31% of the total. With such a small number to supply the vast demand of the country, it is very obvious that it is insufficient. How can there be a phenomenon of overproduction? Even if the people's purchasing power is reduced to below the general level, the phenomenon of reducing working hours due to overproduction will not occur. It can be seen that the yarn factories' reduction in working hours this time is more accurately due to the dumping of foreign goods. Therefore, the current issue is how to resist foreign goods in order to promote national goods, rather than the issue of overproduction and implementing reductions in working hours.

At this time of deepening national crisis and panic, the capital side should share weal and woe with the labor side to overcome this difficult situation. They must never allow the formation of hundreds of thousands of industrial reserve troops due to the relationship of reducing working hours, causing a panic of hunger in society. On the workers' side, they should also unite and use legal means to argue on the basis of reason, and not stop until they achieve their goals. At the same time, the factory should base its spirit of sacrifice, not only should it not reduce working hours, but it should also give workers more work opportunities, so that the production of the entire nation has a significant improvement. Even if there are any difficulties, it may as well use an open attitude, standing on the position of mutual support and interdependence, and jointly request the government to implement protective policies with the power of the state. And urgently arouse the attention of all aspects of society, using the strength of the entire nation to resist the dumping of foreign goods, so that domestic goods can be sold smoothly on the land of the country. At that time, industry and commerce will be unusually developed, the national economy will also be very active, and the lives of workers will naturally be improved. The phenomenon of unemployment due to work stoppages and reductions in working hours will inevitably disappear, never to be seen again.

Page 23

Film Supplement

A Record of Ms. Qiao Sheng's Appearance on the Silver Screen 256

— Cao Wenzhong

| Career Cannot Prevent Love |

From the perspective of ordinary people, it seems that both husband and wife working in the film industry may endanger the happiness of the family, but Al Jolson does not object to his wife, Ruby Keeler, entering the film industry. She was originally the pillar of the Ziegfeld Follies. Since marrying Jolson on September 21, 1928, she has left the stage.

She has signed a long-term contract with Warner Bros. Pictures. The nature of that contract is almost a birthday gift. On August 25, Warner Bros. production manager Darryl Zanuck discussed Keeler's film acting with Jolson and sought his consent. Jolson told him, "Tonight, if you prepare a contract, then tomorrow we will show it to her and it will definitely surprise her, because tomorrow is her birthday and she will be very willing to sign it."

Keeler signed the contract. When filming the first film, she was stipulated to have a weekly salary of $2,000, with subsequent increases in salary. Jolson is his wife's agent and manager. He is very happy with his new task and it arouses his interest.

He said frankly: "Of course, I am very happy that Ruby has the opportunity to appear on the screen, thereby developing her talent. She is very lonely here, often thinking about her stage career in New York. Her only reason is that she is not busy in Hollywood. If she can make movies, it can arouse her interest and make her happy. If she doesn't like making movies, she can leave."

"One thing is real—she will never let her career interfere with our love and our lives. Because she wanted to live with me, she deliberately fell down the stairs when she was acting on the stage. She is an extraordinary woman. She knows what is right and wrong, so I have no doubt that another movie star can be created in our family."

Ruby Keeler does not regard work as a lifelong career. She can join or withdraw immediately. Jolson's income is very rich. He is a generous husband, and regards it as a fresh thing to play with. Al Jolson is very supportive of his wife working in the film industry.

Audience Opinions

Thoughts After Watching "Awakening" 257

— Shi Zeyong

After Youlian Film Company dissolved last winter, Ms. Fan Xuepeng, who was famous for martial arts films, raised funds to open the Qianghua Film Company, and took the position of manager to engage in film production. Now, her first production, "Awakening," has been publicly screened at the Beijing Grand Theater since the day before yesterday (the 19th).

The drama's purpose is to analyze pure love and hypocritical love clearly. It can be a powerful wake-up call for modern young men and women, enlightening young men and women to recognize the true meaning of love. Because modern young men and women are increasingly on the path of depravity, that evil society cannot escape a part of the responsibility for the sin. As in this film: Yulin was tempted by the city, had a new love, and abandoned a poor Meigu, disregarding her. His lack of focus on love simply treated women as playthings. Later, Yulin's property was taken away by Yunxian, and he was left with nothing. He had to beg to Shanghai. At this time, that Meigu, who was truly "when fortune comes, it comes in pairs; when misfortune strikes, it comes alone," had become a dancer, and was also wronged and sentenced to 15 years in prison. After being released from prison, Yulin had already awakened, so he brought her back.

The general public who are immersed in the sea of love, if they still don't quickly "awaken" after watching this film, it is really a disservice to the film's bitter purpose!

This film can alert modern youth and is worthy of our emotion and admiration. Among the actors' performances, Fan Xuepeng, who plays Meigu, is the best. There is also a Yu Guang, whom we have never met, who is also acceptable. In terms of photography, some scenes are too complicated and too blurred. In terms of scenery, other things are fine, only the dance hall scene seems too unrefined. Perhaps this is restricted by capital?

In short, this film is much more successful than the productions of other small companies.

Da Guangming Concert Program 258

— Yun Yan

Appearing on Stage at 9:15 Tonight

The Shanghai Municipal Council String Orchestra is scheduled to hold a Chinese-Western integrated concert at the Da Guangming Cinema at 9:15 this evening (Sunday). Dr. Mei Baiqi will guide the orchestra, and Dr. Mei Lanfang will be invited to introduce it on stage. The program is as follows: (1) Selected Chinese Ancient Music (Datong Concert), (2) Pipa Solo "Huaiyin Pingchu" (Mr. Wei Zhongle), (3) Poetic Song and Play "Qingwen's Last Words" (composed by Mr. Zhu Manxin, sung by Mrs. Liu Jingfang, directed by Dr. Mei Baiqi), (4) Sound Sketch "Impressions of Beijing Hutongs" (Symphonic Poem), (5) Chinese Pantomime "Qin Xin Bo Guang". This play was composed and directed by the Russian composer Afsha Lomov, and sponsored by Dr. Mei Lanfang. The actors are Tianyi Film Company stars Yuan Meiyun and others. It is based on Chinese folk tales, compiled with pentatonic melodies, and is divided into five scenes. The structure is compact, the plot is bizarre, and the movements in the play all imitate the Chinese stage opera program.

Talking About "Powder Market" 259

— Sheng An

Mingxing Film Company has made significant progress recently. The past "Mad Current" and the current "Powder Market" are all contributions that closely follow the times.

In terms of consciousness, "Powder Market" exposes how modern capitalists use "vases" to attract male customers, and also shows how women should create their own future. These are all "modernized" themes, but it is a pity that Gong Jianong's close following of Hu Die at the end is a bit of "adding feet to the snake."

Director Zhang Shichuan has made progress compared to "Lovelorn," but many places that could be depicted are lightly passed over, which is a pity. The flexibility of the division of scenes and the angles of the shots shows that domestic films are progressing.

Speaking of performance, Hu Die's performance is very powerful, delicate and appropriate, and subtle. Gong Jianong is also very successful, but not as powerful as in "Mad Current." Wang Xianzai is also satisfactory. The other supporting roles are performed mediocrely.

The sound is very clear and the dialogue is also very beautiful, but some scenes are too long and dull. It would be better if they could be shorter. The background is artistic and magnificent, giving people aesthetic beauty.

In short, this "Powder Market" is a superior film from Mingxing Film Company.

What I Saw After Watching "New Year's Eve" 260

— Xu Hairong

Recently, Lianhua's new film "New Year's Eve" has been publicly screened in Beijing again. On Saturday afternoon, there are usually no classes at the school, so I rushed to watch it.

However, this film gave me great disappointment. In terms of the script, it cannot be completely in line with the actual situation. Although it had previously shouted for the laboring masses, it later came up with a story of a bourgeois figure saving the poor. The old scholar in the script is righteous and generous, and the money shop owner is charitable. These are all propaganda articles for feudal ideology and traps for the bourgeoisie to oppress the masses. To put it bluntly, it is simply anesthetizing our audience. Such films with bad consciousness are really not taken by us.

Now, let's put aside consciousness and talk about its performance skills. Then this film can be said to be worth watching. Director Jiang Qifeng's technique is very flexible. Every shot is arranged very appropriately, and the picture is very beautiful. Among them, there is a scene in which the dance hall owner and the money shop's collector fight each other on the snow, which is the best shot, but the plot of the whole film does not seem to be tense enough. Originally, "New Year's Eve" is a great tragedy, which has the possibility of making people cry, but in the end, no hot tears flowed from my eyes. This also shows that the film's power to move people is not enough.

Words About "New Year's Eve" 261

— Ni Qiu

The name "New Year's Eve" has already been very artistically titled. After watching it, I feel that the director is the most successful one in this film. Because the story of the entire film is extremely ordinary. If it is said in itself, it is just a "skillful" film, but after the director's efforts, a few powerful shots have been added, and it has become a "powerful" film.

Several shots, such as: the old man's surprised state after getting the wallet, and the performance of rational conflict are all very good. This is due to Liu Jiqun. In addition, like the old man's expression when he couldn't borrow money and saw three hundred yuan when he returned home, it was all very rare. Several close-ups also made people not feel repetitive after watching them.

Huang Shaofen's photography in this film is also much better than before in one scene of Qianghua Film Company's new film "Our Way of Life," co-starring Fan Xuepeng and Yu Guang. The light is very soft, and the scenery is also very realistic. Only the snow scene is too careless. Large pieces fell on the clothes and hats, clearly showing that these were paper pieces. I hope they can be improved in the future.

The actors are generally fine, especially Jiang Junchao. Although many places are over the top (like the performance when throwing himself into the river), things like meeting Chen Yanyan when he returned to the village to collect debts were very natural.

Although there are many places where the plot of "New Year's Eve" deviates from the facts, they have all been lightly covered up by the director's skills.

In summary, "New Year's Eve" is a short, creative film that depicts the ordinary process of life. If the script can be further refined and supplemented, it may become a masterpiece like "Grand Hotel." Therefore, apart from feeling that the consciousness of "New Year's Eve" is not very sound, it can generally be called a "good film."

An Eternal Regret: The Movie Novel (The White Sister) (Part Five) 262

— By En Ping

A Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer Production Starring Helen Hayes

Sacrificing Reputation and Happiness for Love

"Goodbye, Orlandini," she said resolutely.

"My name is Giovanni," he said, smiling, his large hand firmly clasping her slender, jade-like hand.

She shook her head.

"Goodbye, Orlandini," she said again. "I will never forget you!"

"You can be sure you won't forget!" he exclaimed. "Wait a moment!" He bought a bouquet of fresh flowers from a passing flower girl and tucked it into Angela's surprised arm.

"Orlandini, you're crazy!" she said sternly. But her eyes were hazy, as if covered with a layer of mist.

"Naturally, I'm crazy," he agreed readily. "Is he too?"

"Please go," she pleaded, her voice trembling slightly.

"Am I not allowed to enter?" he also implored. Then, he shook his head and asked teasingly, "Ah! This is a garden! When will you allow visitors to enter? Tomorrow? Then, Friday?"

"You can't! You absolutely can't!" she said. But her eyes conveyed another meaning, emitting a seductive sentiment.

He clicked his heels together, gave a military salute, and turned to leave.

"Giovanni!" she called out softly, madly.

"Yes?" he turned back eagerly. She extended her hand. He held her hand again.

"Goodbye," she said very gently.

He still held her hand. Time stood still in that instant. They looked at each other in silence. Then, slowly, reluctantly, they separated. Angela turned and slipped through the large iron gate, hurried up the steps, and darted into the house. She stopped by the porcelain statue of the Virgin Mary, placed the flowers Giovanni had given her at the statue's feet, and whispered happily:

"A young man bought these for me. His name is Giovanni. He said he loves me." Her eyes looked up at the statue, emitting a strange, mysterious glow. Then, suddenly, a shadow of doubt crossed her face. "Was that wrong, was it, was it?" she murmured resentfully. "He is such a handsome young man... If that was wrong..." She made the sign of the cross on her chest and slowly ran downstairs. Her lips moved in prayer. (To be continued)
